\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+MANBRIEF\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+ memory management functions of the CUDA runtime API (\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+CURRENT\+\_\+\+FILE\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+) \+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+ENDMANBRIEF\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+

This section describes the memory management functions of the CUDA runtime application programming interface.

Some functions have overloaded C++ API template versions documented separately in the \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___h_i_g_h_l_e_v_e_l}{C++ API Routines} module.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaArrayGetInfo()}{cudaArrayGetInfo()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Array\+Get\+Info (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{struct}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structcuda_channel_format_desc}{cuda\+Channel\+Format\+Desc}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{desc,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{struct}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structcuda_extent}{cuda\+Extent}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{extent,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{unsigned}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{int}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{flags,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gaaf8b3ba752727d996074a71ee997ce68}{cuda\+Array\+\_\+t}}}]{array }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Gets info about the specified cuda\+Array. 

Returns in {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}desc}, {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}extent} and {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}flags} respectively, the type, shape and flags of {\ttfamily array}.

Any of {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}desc}, {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}extent} and {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}flags} may be specified as NULL.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}

\hline
{\em extent} & -\/ Returned array shape. 2D arrays will have depth of zero \\
\hline
{\em flags} & -\/ Returned array flags \\
\hline
{\em array} & -\/ The \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Array} to get info for\\
\hline

\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaArrayGetMemoryRequirements()}{cudaArrayGetMemoryRequirements()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Array\+Get\+Memory\+Requirements (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{struct}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structcuda_array_memory_requirements}{cuda\+Array\+Memory\+Requirements}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{memory\+Requirements,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gaaf8b3ba752727d996074a71ee997ce68}{cuda\+Array\+\_\+t}}}]{array,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{int}}}]{device }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Returns the memory requirements of a CUDA array. 

Returns the memory requirements of a CUDA array in {\ttfamily memory\+Requirements} If the CUDA array is not allocated with flag \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga91a50795515848406a89c2e6cef2fb02}{cuda\+Array\+Deferred\+Mapping} cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value will be returned.

The returned value in \doxylink{structcuda_array_memory_requirements_acff0bc12daa05c6c40892a2187befd87}{cuda\+Array\+Memory\+Requirements\+::size} represents the total size of the CUDA array. The returned value in \doxylink{structcuda_array_memory_requirements_a37898b13b500d39e4a43d0ee04cf0ef3}{cuda\+Array\+Memory\+Requirements\+::alignment} represents the alignment necessary for mapping the CUDA array.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
cuda\+Success cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value
\end{DoxyReturn}

\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em device} & -\/ Device to get the memory requirements for \\

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaArrayGetPlane()}{cudaArrayGetPlane()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Array\+Get\+Plane (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gaaf8b3ba752727d996074a71ee997ce68}{cuda\+Array\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Plane\+Array,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gaaf8b3ba752727d996074a71ee997ce68}{cuda\+Array\+\_\+t}}}]{h\+Array,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{unsigned}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{int}}}]{plane\+Idx }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Gets a CUDA array plane from a CUDA array. 

Returns in {\ttfamily p\+Plane\+Array} a CUDA array that represents a single format plane of the CUDA array {\ttfamily h\+Array}.

If {\ttfamily plane\+Idx} is greater than the maximum number of planes in this array or if the array does not have a multi-\/planar format e.\+g\+: cuda\+Channel\+Format\+Kind\+NV12, then cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value is returned.

Note that if the {\ttfamily h\+Array} has format cuda\+Channel\+Format\+Kind\+NV12, then passing in 0 for {\ttfamily plane\+Idx} returns a CUDA array of the same size as {\ttfamily h\+Array} but with one 8-\/bit channel and cuda\+Channel\+Format\+Kind\+Unsigned as its format kind. If 1 is passed for {\ttfamily plane\+Idx}, then the returned CUDA array has half the height and width of {\ttfamily h\+Array} with two 8-\/bit channels and cuda\+Channel\+Format\+Kind\+Unsigned as its format kind.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em p\+Plane\+Array} & -\/ Returned CUDA array referenced by the {\ttfamily plane\+Idx} \\
\hline
{\em h\+Array} & -\/ CUDA array \\
\hline
{\em plane\+Idx} & -\/ Plane index\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
cuda\+Success, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Resource\+Handle \textbackslash{}notefnerr
\end{DoxyReturn}

\Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gacdaaf9a0dbebfb484f3acaff9d7c3872}\label{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gacdaaf9a0dbebfb484f3acaff9d7c3872} 
\index{Memory Management@{Memory Management}!cudaArrayGetSparseProperties@{cudaArrayGetSparseProperties}}
\index{cudaArrayGetSparseProperties@{cudaArrayGetSparseProperties}!Memory Management@{Memory Management}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaArrayGetSparseProperties()}{cudaArrayGetSparseProperties()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Array\+Get\+Sparse\+Properties (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{struct}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structcuda_array_sparse_properties}{cuda\+Array\+Sparse\+Properties}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{sparse\+Properties,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gaaf8b3ba752727d996074a71ee997ce68}{cuda\+Array\+\_\+t}}}]{array }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Returns the layout properties of a sparse CUDA array. 

Returns the layout properties of a sparse CUDA array in {\ttfamily sparse\+Properties}. If the CUDA array is not allocated with flag \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga42c353686a15da063dc7722594ae4bff}{cuda\+Array\+Sparse} cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value will be returned.

If the returned value in \doxylink{structcuda_array_sparse_properties_a44c8728469d60e511aceb4ba7086c164}{cuda\+Array\+Sparse\+Properties\+::flags} contains \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga6820071ffa1300699897eab8d319e4d9}{cuda\+Array\+Sparse\+Properties\+Single\+Mip\+Tail}, then \doxylink{structcuda_array_sparse_properties_a22cfa4ad83195f0e9585303c988bb886}{cuda\+Array\+Sparse\+Properties\+::miptail\+Size} represents the total size of the array. Otherwise, it will be zero. Also, the returned value in \doxylink{structcuda_array_sparse_properties_ab6909e5db55b866477b6cc16fb02f9d3}{cuda\+Array\+Sparse\+Properties\+::miptail\+First\+Level} is always zero. Note that the {\ttfamily array} must have been allocated using \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gaae428013daae74529feb93b48a9dc39b}{cuda\+Malloc\+Array} or \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gaf3a3790459bdc37339fff10927ef8214}{cuda\+Malloc3\+DArray}. For CUDA arrays obtained using \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Mipmapped\+Array\+Get\+Level}, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value will be returned. Instead, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga90c9f8622c8b4172a434f2ed2e145a48}{cuda\+Mipmapped\+Array\+Get\+Sparse\+Properties} must be used to obtain the sparse properties of the entire CUDA mipmapped array to which {\ttfamily array} belongs to.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
cuda\+Success cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value
\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em sparse\+Properties} & -\/ Pointer to return the \doxylink{structcuda_array_sparse_properties}{cuda\+Array\+Sparse\+Properties} \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em array} & -\/ The CUDA array to get the sparse properties of\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga90c9f8622c8b4172a434f2ed2e145a48}{cuda\+Mipmapped\+Array\+Get\+Sparse\+Properties}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___v_a_ga2bebaf075ad1fc9288bb78d14b2265dd}{cu\+Mem\+Map\+Array\+Async} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga5635c759c41d1d2ea21fd46bb5744f15}\label{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga5635c759c41d1d2ea21fd46bb5744f15} 
\index{Memory Management@{Memory Management}!cudaFree@{cudaFree}}
\index{cudaFree@{cudaFree}!Memory Management@{Memory Management}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaFree()}{cudaFree()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+cudart\+\_\+builtin\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Free (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{dev\+Ptr }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Frees memory on the device. 

Frees the memory space pointed to by {\ttfamily dev\+Ptr}, which must have been returned by a previous call to \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga2ec57cea7c57e8e3c4beca43dd327134}{cuda\+Malloc()} or \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gafba768d1a49ed27c0672832403544252}{cuda\+Malloc\+Pitch()}. Otherwise, or if \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga5635c759c41d1d2ea21fd46bb5744f15}{cuda\+Free}({\ttfamily dev\+Ptr}) has already been called before, an error is returned. If {\ttfamily dev\+Ptr} is 0, no operation is performed. \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga5635c759c41d1d2ea21fd46bb5744f15}{cuda\+Free()} returns \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Error\+Value} in case of failure.

The device version of \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga5635c759c41d1d2ea21fd46bb5744f15}{cuda\+Free} cannot be used with a {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}dev\+Ptr} allocated using the host API, and vice versa.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em dev\+Ptr} & -\/ Device pointer to memory to free\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
cuda\+Success, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value \textbackslash{}notefnerr \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+init\+\_\+rt \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+callback
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}

\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaGetMipmappedArrayLevel()}{cudaGetMipmappedArrayLevel()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Get\+Mipmapped\+Array\+Level (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gaaf8b3ba752727d996074a71ee997ce68}{cuda\+Array\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{level\+Array,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga3aceb59159273bec67226fc336cd4f69}{cuda\+Mipmapped\+Array\+\_\+const\+\_\+t}}}]{mipmapped\+Array,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{unsigned}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{int}}}]{level }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Gets a mipmap level of a CUDA mipmapped array. 

Returns in {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}level\+Array} a CUDA array that represents a single mipmap level of the CUDA mipmapped array {\ttfamily mipmapped\+Array}.

If {\ttfamily level} is greater than the maximum number of levels in this mipmapped array, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value is returned.

If {\ttfamily mipmapped\+Array} is NULL, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Resource\+Handle is returned.

\end{DoxyParams}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaGetSymbolAddress()}{cudaGetSymbolAddress()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Get\+Symbol\+Address (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{dev\+Ptr,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{symbol }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Finds the address associated with a CUDA symbol. 

Returns in {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}dev\+Ptr} the address of symbol {\ttfamily symbol} on the device. {\ttfamily symbol} is a variable that resides in global or constant memory space. If {\ttfamily symbol} cannot be found, or if {\ttfamily symbol} is not declared in the global or constant memory space, {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}dev\+Ptr} is unchanged and the error cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Symbol is returned.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaGetSymbolSize()}{cudaGetSymbolSize()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Get\+Symbol\+Size (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{size,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{symbol }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}

\index{Memory Management@{Memory Management}!cudaHostAlloc@{cudaHostAlloc}}
\index{cudaHostAlloc@{cudaHostAlloc}!Memory Management@{Memory Management}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaHostAlloc()}{cudaHostAlloc()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Host\+Alloc (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Host,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{size,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{unsigned}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{int}}}]{flags }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Allocates page-\/locked memory on the host. 

Allocates {\ttfamily size} bytes of host memory that is page-\/locked and accessible to the device. The driver tracks the virtual memory ranges allocated with this function and automatically accelerates calls to functions such as \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gae2bbb87e03bde890140dae4b348e1886}{cuda\+Memcpy()}. Since the memory can be accessed directly by the device, it can be read or written with much higher bandwidth than pageable memory obtained with functions such as \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{malloc()}. Allocating excessive amounts of pinned memory may degrade system performance, since it reduces the amount of memory available to the system for paging. As a result, this function is best used sparingly to allocate staging areas for data exchange between host and device.

The {\ttfamily flags} parameter enables different options to be specified that affect the allocation, as follows.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Host\+Alloc\+Default\+:} This flag\textquotesingle{}s value is defined to be 0 and causes \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga82f207b7718d36489753c35ad398a41a}{cuda\+Host\+Alloc()} to emulate \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga9319967aebbae316ea45f540f27974b7}{cuda\+Malloc\+Host()}.
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Host\+Alloc\+Portable\+:} The memory returned by this call will be considered as pinned memory by all CUDA contexts, not just the one that performed the allocation.
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Host\+Alloc\+Mapped\+:} Maps the allocation into the CUDA address space. The device pointer to the memory may be obtained by calling \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gac03e953b51e1011847c199286de44ac9}{cuda\+Host\+Get\+Device\+Pointer()}.
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Host\+Alloc\+Write\+Combined\+:} Allocates the memory as write-\/combined (WC). WC memory can be transferred across the PCI Express bus more quickly on some system configurations, but cannot be read efficiently by most CPUs. WC memory is a good option for buffers that will be written by the CPU and read by the device via mapped pinned memory or host-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}device transfers.
\end{DoxyItemize}

All of these flags are orthogonal to one another\+: a developer may allocate memory that is portable, mapped and/or write-\/combined with no restrictions.

In order for the \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga01e600c738b962c8f973dda7708f7a70}{cuda\+Host\+Alloc\+Mapped} flag to have any effect, the CUDA context must support the \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga3762be9cccdd809a4ca128354fd134b0}{cuda\+Device\+Map\+Host} flag, which can be checked via \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___d_e_v_i_c_e_ga129ea6446f87d512b19990b0fa2f2331}{cuda\+Get\+Device\+Flags()}. The \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga3762be9cccdd809a4ca128354fd134b0}{cuda\+Device\+Map\+Host} flag is implicitly set for contexts created via the runtime API.

The \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga01e600c738b962c8f973dda7708f7a70}{cuda\+Host\+Alloc\+Mapped} flag may be specified on CUDA contexts for devices that do not support mapped pinned memory. The failure is deferred to \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gac03e953b51e1011847c199286de44ac9}{cuda\+Host\+Get\+Device\+Pointer()} because the memory may be mapped into other CUDA contexts via the \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gac46ce76be41cf79774331cc8cfceb52b}{cuda\+Host\+Alloc\+Portable} flag.

Memory allocated by this function must be freed with \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gab2cf81dca6424eaea7dc92c73a7a8743}{cuda\+Free\+Host()}.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em p\+Host} & -\/ Device pointer to allocated memory \\
\hline
{\em size} & -\/ Requested allocation size in bytes \\
\hline
{\em flags} & -\/ Requested properties of allocated memory\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
cuda\+Success, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value, cuda\+Error\+Memory\+Allocation \textbackslash{}notefnerr \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+init\+\_\+rt \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+callback
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___d_e_v_i_c_e_gab07b3a85443eb322b583aa2e79570c28}{cuda\+Set\+Device\+Flags}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga9319967aebbae316ea45f540f27974b7}{cuda\+Malloc\+Host (C API)}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gab2cf81dca6424eaea7dc92c73a7a8743}{cuda\+Free\+Host}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___d_e_v_i_c_e_ga129ea6446f87d512b19990b0fa2f2331}{cuda\+Get\+Device\+Flags}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___m_e_m_gada6927828b81f5415eb0a7cb0134e522}{cu\+Mem\+Host\+Alloc} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gac03e953b51e1011847c199286de44ac9}\label{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gac03e953b51e1011847c199286de44ac9} 
\index{Memory Management@{Memory Management}!cudaHostGetDevicePointer@{cudaHostGetDevicePointer}}
\index{cudaHostGetDevicePointer@{cudaHostGetDevicePointer}!Memory Management@{Memory Management}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaHostGetDevicePointer()}{cudaHostGetDevicePointer()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Host\+Get\+Device\+Pointer (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Device,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Host,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{unsigned}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{int}}}]{flags }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Passes back device pointer of mapped host memory allocated by cuda\+Host\+Alloc or registered by cuda\+Host\+Register. 

Passes back the device pointer corresponding to the mapped, pinned host buffer allocated by \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga82f207b7718d36489753c35ad398a41a}{cuda\+Host\+Alloc()} or registered by \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gab14cbfaca14c4de9d06a5af14c9307f6}{cuda\+Host\+Register()}.

\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gac03e953b51e1011847c199286de44ac9}{cuda\+Host\+Get\+Device\+Pointer()} will fail if the \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga3762be9cccdd809a4ca128354fd134b0}{cuda\+Device\+Map\+Host} flag was not specified before deferred context creation occurred, or if called on a device that does not support mapped, pinned memory.

For devices that have a non-\/zero value for the device attribute cuda\+Dev\+Attr\+Can\+Use\+Host\+Pointer\+For\+Registered\+Mem, the memory can also be accessed from the device using the host pointer {\ttfamily p\+Host}. The device pointer returned by \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gac03e953b51e1011847c199286de44ac9}{cuda\+Host\+Get\+Device\+Pointer()} may or may not match the original host pointer {\ttfamily p\+Host} and depends on the devices visible to the application. If all devices visible to the application have a non-\/zero value for the device attribute, the device pointer returned by \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gac03e953b51e1011847c199286de44ac9}{cuda\+Host\+Get\+Device\+Pointer()} will match the original pointer {\ttfamily p\+Host}. If any device visible to the application has a zero value for the device attribute, the device pointer returned by \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gac03e953b51e1011847c199286de44ac9}{cuda\+Host\+Get\+Device\+Pointer()} will not match the original host pointer {\ttfamily p\+Host}, but it will be suitable for use on all devices provided Unified Virtual Addressing is enabled. In such systems, it is valid to access the memory using either pointer on devices that have a non-\/zero value for the device attribute. Note however that such devices should access the memory using only of the two pointers and not both.

{\ttfamily flags} provides for future releases. For now, it must be set to 0.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em p\+Device} & -\/ Returned device pointer for mapped memory \\
\hline
{\em p\+Host} & -\/ Requested host pointer mapping \\
\hline
{\em flags} & -\/ Flags for extensions (must be 0 for now)\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
cuda\+Success, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value, cuda\+Error\+Memory\+Allocation \textbackslash{}notefnerr \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+init\+\_\+rt \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+callback
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___d_e_v_i_c_e_gab07b3a85443eb322b583aa2e79570c28}{cuda\+Set\+Device\+Flags}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga82f207b7718d36489753c35ad398a41a}{cuda\+Host\+Alloc}, cu\+Mem\+Host\+Get\+Device\+Pointer 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gac3189ebb0c68f656349b4d2614d51032}\label{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gac3189ebb0c68f656349b4d2614d51032} 
\index{Memory Management@{Memory Management}!cudaHostGetFlags@{cudaHostGetFlags}}
\index{cudaHostGetFlags@{cudaHostGetFlags}!Memory Management@{Memory Management}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaHostGetFlags()}{cudaHostGetFlags()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Host\+Get\+Flags (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{unsigned}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{int}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Flags,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Host }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Passes back flags used to allocate pinned host memory allocated by cuda\+Host\+Alloc. 

\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gac3189ebb0c68f656349b4d2614d51032}{cuda\+Host\+Get\+Flags()} will fail if the input pointer does not reside in an address range allocated by \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga82f207b7718d36489753c35ad398a41a}{cuda\+Host\+Alloc()}.

\Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gab14cbfaca14c4de9d06a5af14c9307f6}\label{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gab14cbfaca14c4de9d06a5af14c9307f6} 
\index{Memory Management@{Memory Management}!cudaHostRegister@{cudaHostRegister}}
\index{cudaHostRegister@{cudaHostRegister}!Memory Management@{Memory Management}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaHostRegister()}{cudaHostRegister()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Host\+Register (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{ptr,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{size,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{unsigned}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{int}}}]{flags }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Registers an existing host memory range for use by CUDA. 

Page-\/locks the memory range specified by {\ttfamily ptr} and {\ttfamily size} and maps it for the device(s) as specified by {\ttfamily flags}. This memory range also is added to the same tracking mechanism as \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga82f207b7718d36489753c35ad398a41a}{cuda\+Host\+Alloc()} to automatically accelerate calls to functions such as \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gae2bbb87e03bde890140dae4b348e1886}{cuda\+Memcpy()}. Since the memory can be accessed directly by the device, it can be read or written with much higher bandwidth than pageable memory that has not been registered. Page-\/locking excessive amounts of memory may degrade system performance, since it reduces the amount of memory available to the system for paging. As a result, this function is best used sparingly to register staging areas for data exchange between host and device.

\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gab14cbfaca14c4de9d06a5af14c9307f6}{cuda\+Host\+Register} is supported only on I/O coherent devices that have a non-\/zero value for the device attribute cuda\+Dev\+Attr\+Host\+Register\+Supported.

The {\ttfamily flags} parameter enables different options to be specified that affect the allocation, as follows.


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Host\+Register\+Default\+:} On a system with unified virtual addressing, the memory will be both mapped and portable. On a system with no unified virtual addressing, the memory will be neither mapped nor portable.
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Host\+Register\+Portable\+:} The memory returned by this call will be considered as pinned memory by all CUDA contexts, not just the one that performed the allocation.
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Host\+Register\+Mapped\+:} Maps the allocation into the CUDA address space. The device pointer to the memory may be obtained by calling \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gac03e953b51e1011847c199286de44ac9}{cuda\+Host\+Get\+Device\+Pointer()}.
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Host\+Register\+Io\+Memory\+:} The passed memory pointer is treated as pointing to some memory-\/mapped I/O space, e.\+g. belonging to a third-\/party PCIe device, and it will marked as non cache-\/coherent and contiguous.
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Host\+Register\+Read\+Only\+:} The passed memory pointer is treated as pointing to memory that is considered read-\/only by the device. On platforms without cuda\+Dev\+Attr\+Pageable\+Memory\+Access\+Uses\+Host\+Page\+Tables, this flag is required in order to register memory mapped to the CPU as read-\/only. Support for the use of this flag can be queried from the device attribute cuda\+Device\+Attr\+Read\+Only\+Host\+Register\+Supported. Using this flag with a current context associated with a device that does not have this attribute set will cause \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gab14cbfaca14c4de9d06a5af14c9307f6}{cuda\+Host\+Register} to error with cuda\+Error\+Not\+Supported.
\end{DoxyItemize}

All of these flags are orthogonal to one another\+: a developer may page-\/lock memory that is portable or mapped with no restrictions.

The CUDA context must have been created with the \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Map\+Host} flag in order for the \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga838b73458521c60f502efd19db0e365d}{cuda\+Host\+Register\+Mapped} flag to have any effect.

The \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga838b73458521c60f502efd19db0e365d}{cuda\+Host\+Register\+Mapped} flag may be specified on CUDA contexts for devices that do not support mapped pinned memory. The failure is deferred to \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gac03e953b51e1011847c199286de44ac9}{cuda\+Host\+Get\+Device\+Pointer()} because the memory may be mapped into other CUDA contexts via the \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga36977255e5c778f7e4362d32d6b1cecd}{cuda\+Host\+Register\+Portable} flag.

For devices that have a non-\/zero value for the device attribute cuda\+Dev\+Attr\+Can\+Use\+Host\+Pointer\+For\+Registered\+Mem, the memory can also be accessed from the device using the host pointer {\ttfamily ptr}. The device pointer returned by \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gac03e953b51e1011847c199286de44ac9}{cuda\+Host\+Get\+Device\+Pointer()} may or may not match the original host pointer {\ttfamily ptr} and depends on the devices visible to the application. If all devices visible to the application have a non-\/zero value for the device attribute, the device pointer returned by \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gac03e953b51e1011847c199286de44ac9}{cuda\+Host\+Get\+Device\+Pointer()} will match the original pointer {\ttfamily ptr}. If any device visible to the application has a zero value for the device attribute, the device pointer returned by \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gac03e953b51e1011847c199286de44ac9}{cuda\+Host\+Get\+Device\+Pointer()} will not match the original host pointer {\ttfamily ptr}, but it will be suitable for use on all devices provided Unified Virtual Addressing is enabled. In such systems, it is valid to access the memory using either pointer on devices that have a non-\/zero value for the device attribute. Note however that such devices should access the memory using only of the two pointers and not both.

The memory page-\/locked by this function must be unregistered with \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gaa34734225c1a88e5b14f254fb70b567c}{cuda\+Host\+Unregister()}.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ptr} & -\/ Host pointer to memory to page-\/lock \\
\hline
{\em size} & -\/ Size in bytes of the address range to page-\/lock in bytes \\
\hline
{\em flags} & -\/ Flags for allocation request\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
cuda\+Success, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value, cuda\+Error\+Memory\+Allocation, cuda\+Error\+Host\+Memory\+Already\+Registered, cuda\+Error\+Not\+Supported \textbackslash{}notefnerr \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+init\+\_\+rt \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+callback
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gaa34734225c1a88e5b14f254fb70b567c}{cuda\+Host\+Unregister}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gac3189ebb0c68f656349b4d2614d51032}{cuda\+Host\+Get\+Flags}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gac03e953b51e1011847c199286de44ac9}{cuda\+Host\+Get\+Device\+Pointer}, cu\+Mem\+Host\+Register 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gaa34734225c1a88e5b14f254fb70b567c}\label{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gaa34734225c1a88e5b14f254fb70b567c}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaHostUnregister()}{cudaHostUnregister()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Host\+Unregister (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{ptr }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Unregisters a memory range that was registered with cuda\+Host\+Register. 

Unmaps the memory range whose base address is specified by {\ttfamily ptr}, and makes it pageable again.

The base address must be the same one specified to \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gab14cbfaca14c4de9d06a5af14c9307f6}{cuda\+Host\+Register()}.

\Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga2ec57cea7c57e8e3c4beca43dd327134}\label{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga2ec57cea7c57e8e3c4beca43dd327134} 
\index{Memory Management@{Memory Management}!cudaMalloc@{cudaMalloc}}
\index{cudaMalloc@{cudaMalloc}!Memory Management@{Memory Management}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaMalloc()}{cudaMalloc()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+cudart\+\_\+builtin\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Malloc (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{dev\+Ptr,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{size }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Allocate memory on the device. 

Allocates {\ttfamily size} bytes of linear memory on the device and returns in {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}dev\+Ptr} a pointer to the allocated memory. The allocated memory is suitably aligned for any kind of variable. The memory is not cleared. \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga2ec57cea7c57e8e3c4beca43dd327134}{cuda\+Malloc()} returns cuda\+Error\+Memory\+Allocation in case of failure.

The device version of \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga5635c759c41d1d2ea21fd46bb5744f15}{cuda\+Free} cannot be used with a {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}dev\+Ptr} allocated using the host API, and vice versa.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em dev\+Ptr} & -\/ Pointer to allocated device memory \\
\hline
{\em size} & -\/ Requested allocation size in bytes\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
cuda\+Success, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value, cuda\+Error\+Memory\+Allocation \textbackslash{}notefnerr \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+init\+\_\+rt \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+callback
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gafba768d1a49ed27c0672832403544252}{cuda\+Malloc\+Pitch}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga5635c759c41d1d2ea21fd46bb5744f15}{cuda\+Free}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gaae428013daae74529feb93b48a9dc39b}{cuda\+Malloc\+Array}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga8376778324f52aac68d6a33ec5ce7068}{cuda\+Free\+Array}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga38d900061e670e541cebf5042e0e7739}{cuda\+Malloc3D}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gaf3a3790459bdc37339fff10927ef8214}{cuda\+Malloc3\+DArray}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga9319967aebbae316ea45f540f27974b7}{cuda\+Malloc\+Host (C API)}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gab2cf81dca6424eaea7dc92c73a7a8743}{cuda\+Free\+Host}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga82f207b7718d36489753c35ad398a41a}{cuda\+Host\+Alloc}, cu\+Mem\+Alloc 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga38d900061e670e541cebf5042e0e7739}\label{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga38d900061e670e541cebf5042e0e7739} 
\index{Memory Management@{Memory Management}!cudaMalloc3D@{cudaMalloc3D}}
\index{cudaMalloc3D@{cudaMalloc3D}!Memory Management@{Memory Management}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaMalloc3D()}{cudaMalloc3D()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Malloc3D (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{struct}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structcuda_pitched_ptr}{cuda\+Pitched\+Ptr}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{pitched\+Dev\+Ptr,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{struct}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structcuda_extent}{cuda\+Extent}}}]{extent }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Allocates logical 1D, 2D, or 3D memory objects on the device. 

Allocates at least {\ttfamily width} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} {\ttfamily height} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} {\ttfamily depth} bytes of linear memory on the device and returns a \doxylink{structcuda_pitched_ptr}{cuda\+Pitched\+Ptr} in which {\ttfamily ptr} is a pointer to the allocated memory. The function may pad the allocation to ensure hardware alignment requirements are met. The pitch returned in the {\ttfamily pitch} field of {\ttfamily pitched\+Dev\+Ptr} is the width in bytes of the allocation.

The returned \doxylink{structcuda_pitched_ptr}{cuda\+Pitched\+Ptr} contains additional fields {\ttfamily xsize} and {\ttfamily ysize}, the logical width and height of the allocation, which are equivalent to the {\ttfamily width} and {\ttfamily height} {\ttfamily extent} parameters provided by the programmer during allocation.

For allocations of 2D and 3D objects, it is highly recommended that programmers perform allocations using \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga38d900061e670e541cebf5042e0e7739}{cuda\+Malloc3\+D()} or \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gafba768d1a49ed27c0672832403544252}{cuda\+Malloc\+Pitch()}. Due to alignment restrictions in the hardware, this is especially true if the application will be performing memory copies involving 2D or 3D objects (whether linear memory or CUDA arrays).


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em pitched\+Dev\+Ptr} & -\/ Pointer to allocated pitched device memory \\
\hline
{\em extent} & -\/ Requested allocation size ({\ttfamily width} field in bytes)\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
cuda\+Success, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value, cuda\+Error\+Memory\+Allocation \textbackslash{}notefnerr \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+init\+\_\+rt \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+callback
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gafba768d1a49ed27c0672832403544252}{cuda\+Malloc\+Pitch}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga5635c759c41d1d2ea21fd46bb5744f15}{cuda\+Free}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga60a55856b9b01a0620ca1c657debed53}{cuda\+Memcpy3D}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga2c9bdd7406ea3a1215ca4f2bf9e3681f}{cuda\+Memset3D}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gaf3a3790459bdc37339fff10927ef8214}{cuda\+Malloc3\+DArray}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gaae428013daae74529feb93b48a9dc39b}{cuda\+Malloc\+Array}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga8376778324f52aac68d6a33ec5ce7068}{cuda\+Free\+Array}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga9319967aebbae316ea45f540f27974b7}{cuda\+Malloc\+Host (C API)}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gab2cf81dca6424eaea7dc92c73a7a8743}{cuda\+Free\+Host}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga82f207b7718d36489753c35ad398a41a}{cuda\+Host\+Alloc}, make\+\_\+cuda\+Pitched\+Ptr, make\+\_\+cuda\+Extent, cu\+Mem\+Alloc\+Pitch 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gaf3a3790459bdc37339fff10927ef8214}\label{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gaf3a3790459bdc37339fff10927ef8214} 
\index{Memory Management@{Memory Management}!cudaMalloc3DArray@{cudaMalloc3DArray}}
\index{cudaMalloc3DArray@{cudaMalloc3DArray}!Memory Management@{Memory Management}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaMalloc3DArray()}{cudaMalloc3DArray()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Malloc3\+DArray (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gaaf8b3ba752727d996074a71ee997ce68}{cuda\+Array\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{array,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{struct}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structcuda_channel_format_desc}{cuda\+Channel\+Format\+Desc}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{desc,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{struct}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structcuda_extent}{cuda\+Extent}}}]{extent,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{unsigned}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{int}} flags }]{\+\_\+\+\_\+dv0 }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Allocate an array on the device. 

Allocates a CUDA array according to the \doxylink{structcuda_channel_format_desc}{cuda\+Channel\+Format\+Desc} structure {\ttfamily desc} and returns a handle to the new CUDA array in {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}array}.

The \doxylink{structcuda_channel_format_desc}{cuda\+Channel\+Format\+Desc} is defined as\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{struct\ }\mbox{\hyperlink{structcuda_channel_format_desc}{cudaChannelFormatDesc}}\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{structcuda_channel_format_desc_a70dede802100e2acd9f334326e9d7926}{x}},\ \mbox{\hyperlink{structcuda_channel_format_desc_a6570793c6567d0c704e8e8943ccaec43}{y}},\ \mbox{\hyperlink{structcuda_channel_format_desc_ae371d37d940d2397139b0a3b7302f51a}{z}},\ \mbox{\hyperlink{structcuda_channel_format_desc_a06089c5a407a2cbd6ea05e5a39b19d69}{w}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keyword}{enum}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga4cf131513bd90cc6561902e68d6ee3ad}{cudaChannelFormatKind}}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{structcuda_channel_format_desc_a7d561d361936688eeae79c3184698278}{f}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\};}

\end{DoxyCode}
 where \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga4cf131513bd90cc6561902e68d6ee3ad}{cuda\+Channel\+Format\+Kind} is one of cuda\+Channel\+Format\+Kind\+Signed, cuda\+Channel\+Format\+Kind\+Unsigned, or cuda\+Channel\+Format\+Kind\+Float.

\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gaf3a3790459bdc37339fff10927ef8214}{cuda\+Malloc3\+DArray()} can allocate the following\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item A 1D array is allocated if the height and depth extents are both zero.
\item A 2D array is allocated if only the depth extent is zero.
\item A 3D array is allocated if all three extents are non-\/zero.
\item A 1D layered CUDA array is allocated if only the height extent is zero and the cuda\+Array\+Layered flag is set. Each layer is a 1D array. The number of layers is determined by the depth extent.
\item A 2D layered CUDA array is allocated if all three extents are non-\/zero and the cuda\+Array\+Layered flag is set. Each layer is a 2D array. The number of layers is determined by the depth extent.
\item A cubemap CUDA array is allocated if all three extents are non-\/zero and the cuda\+Array\+Cubemap flag is set. Width must be equal to height, and depth must be six. A cubemap is a special type of 2D layered CUDA array, where the six layers represent the six faces of a cube. The order of the six layers in memory is the same as that listed in \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gaa11cdc62ba9e58fb5385f3b9d181c401}{cuda\+Graphics\+Cube\+Face}.
\item A cubemap layered CUDA array is allocated if all three extents are non-\/zero, and both, cuda\+Array\+Cubemap and cuda\+Array\+Layered flags are set. Width must be equal to height, and depth must be a multiple of six. A cubemap layered CUDA array is a special type of 2D layered CUDA array that consists of a collection of cubemaps. The first six layers represent the first cubemap, the next six layers form the second cubemap, and so on.
\end{DoxyItemize}

The {\ttfamily flags} parameter enables different options to be specified that affect the allocation, as follows.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Array\+Default\+:} This flag\textquotesingle{}s value is defined to be 0 and provides default array allocation
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Array\+Layered\+:} Allocates a layered CUDA array, with the depth extent indicating the number of layers
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Array\+Cubemap\+:} Allocates a cubemap CUDA array. Width must be equal to height, and depth must be six. If the cuda\+Array\+Layered flag is also set, depth must be a multiple of six.
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Array\+Surface\+Load\+Store\+:} Allocates a CUDA array that could be read from or written to using a surface reference.
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Array\+Texture\+Gather\+:} This flag indicates that texture gather operations will be performed on the CUDA array. Texture gather can only be performed on 2D CUDA arrays.
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Array\+Sparse\+:} Allocates a CUDA array without physical backing memory. The subregions within this sparse array can later be mapped onto a physical memory allocation by calling \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___v_a_ga2bebaf075ad1fc9288bb78d14b2265dd}{cu\+Mem\+Map\+Array\+Async}. This flag can only be used for creating 2D, 3D or 2D layered sparse CUDA arrays. The physical backing memory must be allocated via \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___v_a_gab5a09e3aee547c0d1d4e8e20a72d7aa3}{cu\+Mem\+Create}.
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Array\+Deferred\+Mapping\+:} Allocates a CUDA array without physical backing memory. The entire array can later be mapped onto a physical memory allocation by calling \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___v_a_ga2bebaf075ad1fc9288bb78d14b2265dd}{cu\+Mem\+Map\+Array\+Async}. The physical backing memory must be allocated via \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___v_a_gab5a09e3aee547c0d1d4e8e20a72d7aa3}{cu\+Mem\+Create}.
\end{DoxyItemize}

The width, height and depth extents must meet certain size requirements as listed in the following table. All values are specified in elements.

Note that 2D CUDA arrays have different size requirements if the \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga142b19a14d56a03b1e410430aa5202d1}{cuda\+Array\+Texture\+Gather} flag is set. In that case, the valid range for (width, height, depth) is ((1,max\+Texture2\+DGather\mbox{[}0\mbox{]}), (1,max\+Texture2\+DGather\mbox{[}1\mbox{]}), 0).

\hline

\hline
{\em extent} & -\/ Requested allocation size ({\ttfamily width} field in elements) \\
\hline
{\em flags} & -\/ Flags for extensions\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\end{DoxyReturn}

\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaMallocArray()}{cudaMallocArray()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Malloc\+Array (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gaaf8b3ba752727d996074a71ee997ce68}{cuda\+Array\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{array,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{struct}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structcuda_channel_format_desc}{cuda\+Channel\+Format\+Desc}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{desc,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{width,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}} height }]{\+\_\+\+\_\+dv0,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{unsigned}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{int}} flags }]{\+\_\+\+\_\+dv0 }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Allocate an array on the device. 

Allocates a CUDA array according to the \doxylink{structcuda_channel_format_desc}{cuda\+Channel\+Format\+Desc} structure {\ttfamily desc} and returns a handle to the new CUDA array in {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}array}.

The \doxylink{structcuda_channel_format_desc}{cuda\+Channel\+Format\+Desc} is defined as\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{struct\ }\mbox{\hyperlink{structcuda_channel_format_desc}{cudaChannelFormatDesc}}\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{structcuda_channel_format_desc_a70dede802100e2acd9f334326e9d7926}{x}},\ \mbox{\hyperlink{structcuda_channel_format_desc_a6570793c6567d0c704e8e8943ccaec43}{y}},\ \mbox{\hyperlink{structcuda_channel_format_desc_ae371d37d940d2397139b0a3b7302f51a}{z}},\ \mbox{\hyperlink{structcuda_channel_format_desc_a06089c5a407a2cbd6ea05e5a39b19d69}{w}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{enum}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga4cf131513bd90cc6561902e68d6ee3ad}{cudaChannelFormatKind}}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{structcuda_channel_format_desc_a7d561d361936688eeae79c3184698278}{f}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\};}

\end{DoxyCode}
 where \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga4cf131513bd90cc6561902e68d6ee3ad}{cuda\+Channel\+Format\+Kind} is one of cuda\+Channel\+Format\+Kind\+Signed, cuda\+Channel\+Format\+Kind\+Unsigned, or cuda\+Channel\+Format\+Kind\+Float.

The {\ttfamily flags} parameter enables different options to be specified that affect the allocation, as follows.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Array\+Default\+:} This flag\textquotesingle{}s value is defined to be 0 and provides default array allocation
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Array\+Surface\+Load\+Store\+:} Allocates an array that can be read from or written to using a surface reference
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Array\+Texture\+Gather\+:} This flag indicates that texture gather operations will be performed on the array.
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Array\+Sparse\+:} Allocates a CUDA array without physical backing memory. The subregions within this sparse array can later be mapped onto a physical memory allocation by calling \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___v_a_ga2bebaf075ad1fc9288bb78d14b2265dd}{cu\+Mem\+Map\+Array\+Async}. The physical backing memory must be allocated via \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___v_a_gab5a09e3aee547c0d1d4e8e20a72d7aa3}{cu\+Mem\+Create}.
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Array\+Deferred\+Mapping\+:} Allocates a CUDA array without physical backing memory. The entire array can later be mapped onto a physical memory allocation by calling \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___v_a_ga2bebaf075ad1fc9288bb78d14b2265dd}{cu\+Mem\+Map\+Array\+Async}. The physical backing memory must be allocated via \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___v_a_gab5a09e3aee547c0d1d4e8e20a72d7aa3}{cu\+Mem\+Create}.
\end{DoxyItemize}

{\ttfamily width} and {\ttfamily height} must meet certain size requirements. See \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gaf3a3790459bdc37339fff10927ef8214}{cuda\+Malloc3\+DArray()} for more details.

\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga2ec57cea7c57e8e3c4beca43dd327134}{cuda\+Malloc}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gafba768d1a49ed27c0672832403544252}{cuda\+Malloc\+Pitch}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga5635c759c41d1d2ea21fd46bb5744f15}{cuda\+Free}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga8376778324f52aac68d6a33ec5ce7068}{cuda\+Free\+Array}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga9319967aebbae316ea45f540f27974b7}{cuda\+Malloc\+Host (C API)}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gab2cf81dca6424eaea7dc92c73a7a8743}{cuda\+Free\+Host}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga38d900061e670e541cebf5042e0e7739}{cuda\+Malloc3D}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gaf3a3790459bdc37339fff10927ef8214}{cuda\+Malloc3\+DArray}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga82f207b7718d36489753c35ad398a41a}{cuda\+Host\+Alloc}, cu\+Array\+Create 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga9319967aebbae316ea45f540f27974b7}\label{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga9319967aebbae316ea45f540f27974b7} 
\index{Memory Management@{Memory Management}!cudaMallocHost@{cudaMallocHost}}
\index{cudaMallocHost@{cudaMallocHost}!Memory Management@{Memory Management}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaMallocHost()}{cudaMallocHost()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Malloc\+Host (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{ptr,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{size }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Allocates page-\/locked memory on the host. 

Allocates {\ttfamily size} bytes of host memory that is page-\/locked and accessible to the device. The driver tracks the virtual memory ranges allocated with this function and automatically accelerates calls to functions such as \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gae2bbb87e03bde890140dae4b348e1886}{cuda\+Memcpy}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}(). Since the memory can be accessed directly by the device, it can be read or written with much higher bandwidth than pageable memory obtained with functions such as \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{malloc()}. Allocating excessive amounts of memory with \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga9319967aebbae316ea45f540f27974b7}{cuda\+Malloc\+Host()} may degrade system performance, since it reduces the amount of memory available to the system for paging. As a result, this function is best used sparingly to allocate staging areas for data exchange between host and device.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ptr} & -\/ Pointer to allocated host memory \\
\hline
{\em size} & -\/ Requested allocation size in bytes\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
cuda\+Success, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value, cuda\+Error\+Memory\+Allocation \textbackslash{}notefnerr \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+init\+\_\+rt \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+callback
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}

\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gac85541d7e0fa6bdaeed967fee1c8e780}\label{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gac85541d7e0fa6bdaeed967fee1c8e780} 
\index{Memory Management@{Memory Management}!cudaMallocManaged@{cudaMallocManaged}}
\index{cudaMallocManaged@{cudaMallocManaged}!Memory Management@{Memory Management}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaMallocManaged()}{cudaMallocManaged()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+cudart\+\_\+builtin\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Malloc\+Managed (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{dev\+Ptr,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{size,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{unsigned}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{int}}}]{flags }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Allocates memory that will be automatically managed by the Unified Memory system. 

Allocates {\ttfamily size} bytes of managed memory on the device and returns in {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}dev\+Ptr} a pointer to the allocated memory. If the device doesn\textquotesingle{}t support allocating managed memory, cuda\+Error\+Not\+Supported is returned. Support for managed memory can be queried using the device attribute cuda\+Dev\+Attr\+Managed\+Memory. The allocated memory is suitably aligned for any kind of variable. The memory is not cleared. If {\ttfamily size} is 0, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gac85541d7e0fa6bdaeed967fee1c8e780}{cuda\+Malloc\+Managed} returns cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value. The pointer is valid on the CPU and on all GPUs in the system that support managed memory. All accesses to this pointer must obey the Unified Memory programming model.

{\ttfamily flags} specifies the default stream association for this allocation. {\ttfamily flags} must be one of \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga4808e47eba73eb94622ec70a9f9b91ff}{cuda\+Mem\+Attach\+Global} or \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga4f9a428d18fdd89a99441d0dd27131c0}{cuda\+Mem\+Attach\+Host}. The default value for {\ttfamily flags} is \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga4808e47eba73eb94622ec70a9f9b91ff}{cuda\+Mem\+Attach\+Global}. If \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga4808e47eba73eb94622ec70a9f9b91ff}{cuda\+Mem\+Attach\+Global} is specified, then this memory is accessible from any stream on any device. If \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga4f9a428d18fdd89a99441d0dd27131c0}{cuda\+Mem\+Attach\+Host} is specified, then the allocation should not be accessed from devices that have a zero value for the device attribute cuda\+Dev\+Attr\+Concurrent\+Managed\+Access; an explicit call to \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___s_t_r_e_a_m_gab873a3bc43def9456d72f9561fe79e65}{cuda\+Stream\+Attach\+Mem\+Async} will be required to enable access on such devices.

If the association is later changed via \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___s_t_r_e_a_m_gab873a3bc43def9456d72f9561fe79e65}{cuda\+Stream\+Attach\+Mem\+Async} to a single stream, the default association, as specifed during \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gac85541d7e0fa6bdaeed967fee1c8e780}{cuda\+Malloc\+Managed}, is restored when that stream is destroyed. For {\bfseries{managed}} variables, the default association is always \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga4808e47eba73eb94622ec70a9f9b91ff}{cuda\+Mem\+Attach\+Global}. Note that destroying a stream is an asynchronous operation, and as a result, the change to default association won\textquotesingle{}t happen until all work in the stream has completed.

Memory allocated with \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gac85541d7e0fa6bdaeed967fee1c8e780}{cuda\+Malloc\+Managed} should be released with \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga5635c759c41d1d2ea21fd46bb5744f15}{cuda\+Free}.

Device memory oversubscription is possible for GPUs that have a non-\/zero value for the device attribute cuda\+Dev\+Attr\+Concurrent\+Managed\+Access. Managed memory on such GPUs may be evicted from device memory to host memory at any time by the Unified Memory driver in order to make room for other allocations.

In a multi-\/\+GPU system where all GPUs have a non-\/zero value for the device attribute cuda\+Dev\+Attr\+Concurrent\+Managed\+Access, managed memory may not be populated when this API returns and instead may be populated on access. In such systems, managed memory can migrate to any processor\textquotesingle{}s memory at any time. The Unified Memory driver will employ heuristics to maintain data locality and prevent excessive page faults to the extent possible. The application can also guide the driver about memory usage patterns via \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gac45d3db8ba1c1387396174838fd7dfad}{cuda\+Mem\+Advise}. The application can also explicitly migrate memory to a desired processor\textquotesingle{}s memory via \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga4a666ced2163d18849c59c608bfbd208}{cuda\+Mem\+Prefetch\+Async}.

In a multi-\/\+GPU system where all of the GPUs have a zero value for the device attribute cuda\+Dev\+Attr\+Concurrent\+Managed\+Access and all the GPUs have peer-\/to-\/peer support with each other, the physical storage for managed memory is created on the GPU which is active at the time \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gac85541d7e0fa6bdaeed967fee1c8e780}{cuda\+Malloc\+Managed} is called. All other GPUs will reference the data at reduced bandwidth via peer mappings over the PCIe bus. The Unified Memory driver does not migrate memory among such GPUs.

In a multi-\/\+GPU system where not all GPUs have peer-\/to-\/peer support with each other and where the value of the device attribute cuda\+Dev\+Attr\+Concurrent\+Managed\+Access is zero for at least one of those GPUs, the location chosen for physical storage of managed memory is system-\/dependent.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item On Linux, the location chosen will be device memory as long as the current set of active contexts are on devices that either have peer-\/to-\/peer support with each other or have a non-\/zero value for the device attribute cuda\+Dev\+Attr\+Concurrent\+Managed\+Access. If there is an active context on a GPU that does not have a non-\/zero value for that device attribute and it does not have peer-\/to-\/peer support with the other devices that have active contexts on them, then the location for physical storage will be \textquotesingle{}zero-\/copy\textquotesingle{} or host memory. Note that this means that managed memory that is located in device memory is migrated to host memory if a new context is created on a GPU that doesn\textquotesingle{}t have a non-\/zero value for the device attribute and does not support peer-\/to-\/peer with at least one of the other devices that has an active context. This in turn implies that context creation may fail if there is insufficient host memory to migrate all managed allocations.
\item On Windows, the physical storage is always created in \textquotesingle{}zero-\/copy\textquotesingle{} or host memory. All GPUs will reference the data at reduced bandwidth over the PCIe bus. In these circumstances, use of the environment variable CUDA\+\_\+\+VISIBLE\+\_\+\+DEVICES is recommended to restrict CUDA to only use those GPUs that have peer-\/to-\/peer support. Alternatively, users can also set CUDA\+\_\+\+MANAGED\+\_\+\+FORCE\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+ALLOC to a non-\/zero value to force the driver to always use device memory for physical storage. When this environment variable is set to a non-\/zero value, all devices used in that process that support managed memory have to be peer-\/to-\/peer compatible with each other. The error cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Device will be returned if a device that supports managed memory is used and it is not peer-\/to-\/peer compatible with any of the other managed memory supporting devices that were previously used in that process, even if \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___d_e_v_i_c_e_gadf472c0854e8464c58659e2bde63eee9}{cuda\+Device\+Reset} has been called on those devices. These environment variables are described in the CUDA programming guide under the "{}\+CUDA environment variables"{} section.
\end{DoxyItemize}
