\index{Memory Management@{Memory Management}!cudaMallocMipmappedArray@{cudaMallocMipmappedArray}}
\index{cudaMallocMipmappedArray@{cudaMallocMipmappedArray}!Memory Management@{Memory Management}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaMallocMipmappedArray()}{cudaMallocMipmappedArray()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Malloc\+Mipmapped\+Array (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga1b03ad14fc0ab86f8b033837f5562d8a}{cuda\+Mipmapped\+Array\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{mipmapped\+Array,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{struct}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structcuda_channel_format_desc}{cuda\+Channel\+Format\+Desc}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{desc,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{struct}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structcuda_extent}{cuda\+Extent}}}]{extent,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{unsigned}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{int}}}]{num\+Levels,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{unsigned}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{int}} flags }]{\+\_\+\+\_\+dv0 }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Allocate a mipmapped array on the device. 

Allocates a CUDA mipmapped array according to the \doxylink{structcuda_channel_format_desc}{cuda\+Channel\+Format\+Desc} structure {\ttfamily desc} and returns a handle to the new CUDA mipmapped array in {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}mipmapped\+Array}. {\ttfamily num\+Levels} specifies the number of mipmap levels to be allocated. This value is clamped to the range \mbox{[}1, 1 + floor(log2(max(width, height, depth)))\mbox{]}.

The \doxylink{structcuda_channel_format_desc}{cuda\+Channel\+Format\+Desc} is defined as\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{struct\ }\mbox{\hyperlink{structcuda_channel_format_desc}{cudaChannelFormatDesc}}\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{structcuda_channel_format_desc_a70dede802100e2acd9f334326e9d7926}{x}},\ \mbox{\hyperlink{structcuda_channel_format_desc_a6570793c6567d0c704e8e8943ccaec43}{y}},\ \mbox{\hyperlink{structcuda_channel_format_desc_ae371d37d940d2397139b0a3b7302f51a}{z}},\ \mbox{\hyperlink{structcuda_channel_format_desc_a06089c5a407a2cbd6ea05e5a39b19d69}{w}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keyword}{enum}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga4cf131513bd90cc6561902e68d6ee3ad}{cudaChannelFormatKind}}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{structcuda_channel_format_desc_a7d561d361936688eeae79c3184698278}{f}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\};}

\end{DoxyCode}
 where \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga4cf131513bd90cc6561902e68d6ee3ad}{cuda\+Channel\+Format\+Kind} is one of cuda\+Channel\+Format\+Kind\+Signed, cuda\+Channel\+Format\+Kind\+Unsigned, or cuda\+Channel\+Format\+Kind\+Float.

\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gabbd44cd19b47353226575a86c6c5be83}{cuda\+Malloc\+Mipmapped\+Array()} can allocate the following\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item A 1D mipmapped array is allocated if the height and depth extents are both zero.
\item A 2D mipmapped array is allocated if only the depth extent is zero.
\item A 3D mipmapped array is allocated if all three extents are non-\/zero.
\item A 1D layered CUDA mipmapped array is allocated if only the height extent is zero and the cuda\+Array\+Layered flag is set. Each layer is a 1D mipmapped array. The number of layers is determined by the depth extent.
\item A 2D layered CUDA mipmapped array is allocated if all three extents are non-\/zero and the cuda\+Array\+Layered flag is set. Each layer is a 2D mipmapped array. The number of layers is determined by the depth extent.
\item A cubemap CUDA mipmapped array is allocated if all three extents are non-\/zero and the cuda\+Array\+Cubemap flag is set. Width must be equal to height, and depth must be six. The order of the six layers in memory is the same as that listed in \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gaa11cdc62ba9e58fb5385f3b9d181c401}{cuda\+Graphics\+Cube\+Face}.
\item A cubemap layered CUDA mipmapped array is allocated if all three extents are non-\/zero, and both, cuda\+Array\+Cubemap and cuda\+Array\+Layered flags are set. Width must be equal to height, and depth must be a multiple of six. A cubemap layered CUDA mipmapped array is a special type of 2D layered CUDA mipmapped array that consists of a collection of cubemap mipmapped arrays. The first six layers represent the first cubemap mipmapped array, the next six layers form the second cubemap mipmapped array, and so on.
\end{DoxyItemize}

The {\ttfamily flags} parameter enables different options to be specified that affect the allocation, as follows.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Array\+Default\+:} This flag\textquotesingle{}s value is defined to be 0 and provides default mipmapped array allocation
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Array\+Layered\+:} Allocates a layered CUDA mipmapped array, with the depth extent indicating the number of layers
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Array\+Cubemap\+:} Allocates a cubemap CUDA mipmapped array. Width must be equal to height, and depth must be six. If the cuda\+Array\+Layered flag is also set, depth must be a multiple of six.
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Array\+Surface\+Load\+Store\+:} This flag indicates that individual mipmap levels of the CUDA mipmapped array will be read from or written to using a surface reference.
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Array\+Texture\+Gather\+:} This flag indicates that texture gather operations will be performed on the CUDA array. Texture gather can only be performed on 2D CUDA mipmapped arrays, and the gather operations are performed only on the most detailed mipmap level.
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Array\+Sparse\+:} Allocates a CUDA mipmapped array without physical backing memory. The subregions within this sparse array can later be mapped onto a physical memory allocation by calling \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___v_a_ga2bebaf075ad1fc9288bb78d14b2265dd}{cu\+Mem\+Map\+Array\+Async}. This flag can only be used for creating 2D, 3D or 2D layered sparse CUDA mipmapped arrays. The physical backing memory must be allocated via \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___v_a_gab5a09e3aee547c0d1d4e8e20a72d7aa3}{cu\+Mem\+Create}.
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Array\+Deferred\+Mapping\+:} Allocates a CUDA mipmapped array without physical backing memory. The entire array can later be mapped onto a physical memory allocation by calling \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___v_a_ga2bebaf075ad1fc9288bb78d14b2265dd}{cu\+Mem\+Map\+Array\+Async}. The physical backing memory must be allocated via \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___v_a_gab5a09e3aee547c0d1d4e8e20a72d7aa3}{cu\+Mem\+Create}.
\end{DoxyItemize}

The width, height and depth extents must meet certain size requirements as listed in the following table. All values are specified in elements.




\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mipmapped\+Array} & -\/ Pointer to allocated mipmapped array in device memory \\
\hline
{\em desc} & -\/ Requested channel format \\
\hline
{\em extent} & -\/ Requested allocation size ({\ttfamily width} field in elements) \\
\hline
{\em num\+Levels} & -\/ Number of mipmap levels to allocate \\
\hline
{\em flags} & -\/ Flags for extensions\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga38d900061e670e541cebf5042e0e7739}{cuda\+Malloc3D}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga2ec57cea7c57e8e3c4beca43dd327134}{cuda\+Malloc}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gafba768d1a49ed27c0672832403544252}{cuda\+Malloc\+Pitch}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga5635c759c41d1d2ea21fd46bb5744f15}{cuda\+Free}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga8376778324f52aac68d6a33ec5ce7068}{cuda\+Free\+Array}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga9319967aebbae316ea45f540f27974b7}{cuda\+Malloc\+Host (C API)}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gab2cf81dca6424eaea7dc92c73a7a8743}{cuda\+Free\+Host}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga82f207b7718d36489753c35ad398a41a}{cuda\+Host\+Alloc}, make\+\_\+cuda\+Extent, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___m_e_m_ga2194e4f8117e242cc371ded1abb054e4}{cu\+Mipmapped\+Array\+Create} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\index{cudaMallocPitch@{cudaMallocPitch}!Memory Management@{Memory Management}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaMallocPitch()}{cudaMallocPitch()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Malloc\+Pitch (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{dev\+Ptr,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{pitch,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{width,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{height }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Allocates pitched memory on the device. 

Allocates at least {\ttfamily width} (in bytes) \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} {\ttfamily height} bytes of linear memory on the device and returns in {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}dev\+Ptr} a pointer to the allocated memory. The function may pad the allocation to ensure that corresponding pointers in any given row will continue to meet the alignment requirements for coalescing as the address is updated from row to row. The pitch returned in {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}pitch} by \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gafba768d1a49ed27c0672832403544252}{cuda\+Malloc\+Pitch()} is the width in bytes of the allocation. The intended usage of {\ttfamily pitch} is as a separate parameter of the allocation, used to compute addresses within the 2D array. Given the row and column of an array element of type {\ttfamily T}, the address is computed as\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{T}}*\ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{pElement}}\ =\ (\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{T}}*)((\textcolor{keywordtype}{char}*)\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{BaseAddress}}\ +\ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{Row}}\ *\ pitch)\ +\ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{Column}};}

\end{DoxyCode}


For allocations of 2D arrays, it is recommended that programmers consider performing pitch allocations using \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gafba768d1a49ed27c0672832403544252}{cuda\+Malloc\+Pitch()}. Due to pitch alignment restrictions in the hardware, this is especially true if the application will be performing 2D memory copies between different regions of device memory (whether linear memory or CUDA arrays).


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em dev\+Ptr} & -\/ Pointer to allocated pitched device memory \\
\hline
{\em pitch} & -\/ Pitch for allocation \\
\hline
{\em width} & -\/ Requested pitched allocation width (in bytes) \\
\hline
{\em height} & -\/ Requested pitched allocation height\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
cuda\+Success, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value, cuda\+Error\+Memory\+Allocation \textbackslash{}notefnerr \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+init\+\_\+rt \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+callback
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga2ec57cea7c57e8e3c4beca43dd327134}{cuda\+Malloc}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga5635c759c41d1d2ea21fd46bb5744f15}{cuda\+Free}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gaae428013daae74529feb93b48a9dc39b}{cuda\+Malloc\+Array}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga8376778324f52aac68d6a33ec5ce7068}{cuda\+Free\+Array}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga9319967aebbae316ea45f540f27974b7}{cuda\+Malloc\+Host (C API)}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gab2cf81dca6424eaea7dc92c73a7a8743}{cuda\+Free\+Host}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga38d900061e670e541cebf5042e0e7739}{cuda\+Malloc3D}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gaf3a3790459bdc37339fff10927ef8214}{cuda\+Malloc3\+DArray}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga82f207b7718d36489753c35ad398a41a}{cuda\+Host\+Alloc}, cu\+Mem\+Alloc\+Pitch 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gac45d3db8ba1c1387396174838fd7dfad}\label{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gac45d3db8ba1c1387396174838fd7dfad} 
\index{Memory Management@{Memory Management}!cudaMemAdvise@{cudaMemAdvise}}
\index{cudaMemAdvise@{cudaMemAdvise}!Memory Management@{Memory Management}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaMemAdvise()}{cudaMemAdvise()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Mem\+Advise (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{dev\+Ptr,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{count,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{enum}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga88409663f456aefb192975278a8b5b3a}{cuda\+Memory\+Advise}}}]{advice,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{int}}}]{device }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Advise about the usage of a given memory range. 

Advise the Unified Memory subsystem about the usage pattern for the memory range starting at {\ttfamily dev\+Ptr} with a size of {\ttfamily count} bytes. The start address and end address of the memory range will be rounded down and rounded up respectively to be aligned to CPU page size before the advice is applied. The memory range must refer to managed memory allocated via \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gac85541d7e0fa6bdaeed967fee1c8e780}{cuda\+Malloc\+Managed} or declared via {\bfseries{managed}} variables. The memory range could also refer to system-\/allocated pageable memory provided it represents a valid, host-\/accessible region of memory and all additional constraints imposed by {\ttfamily advice} as outlined below are also satisfied. Specifying an invalid system-\/allocated pageable memory range results in an error being returned.

The {\ttfamily advice} parameter can take the following values\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Mem\+Advise\+Set\+Read\+Mostly\+:} This implies that the data is mostly going to be read from and only occasionally written to. Any read accesses from any processor to this region will create a read-\/only copy of at least the accessed pages in that processor\textquotesingle{}s memory. Additionally, if \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga4a666ced2163d18849c59c608bfbd208}{cuda\+Mem\+Prefetch\+Async} is called on this region, it will create a read-\/only copy of the data on the destination processor. If any processor writes to this region, all copies of the corresponding page will be invalidated except for the one where the write occurred. The {\ttfamily device} argument is ignored for this advice. Note that for a page to be read-\/duplicated, the accessing processor must either be the CPU or a GPU that has a non-\/zero value for the device attribute cuda\+Dev\+Attr\+Concurrent\+Managed\+Access. Also, if a context is created on a device that does not have the device attribute cuda\+Dev\+Attr\+Concurrent\+Managed\+Access set, then read-\/duplication will not occur until all such contexts are destroyed. If the memory region refers to valid system-\/allocated pageable memory, then the accessing device must have a non-\/zero value for the device attribute cuda\+Dev\+Attr\+Pageable\+Memory\+Access for a read-\/only copy to be created on that device. Note however that if the accessing device also has a non-\/zero value for the device attribute cuda\+Dev\+Attr\+Pageable\+Memory\+Access\+Uses\+Host\+Page\+Tables, then setting this advice will not create a read-\/only copy when that device accesses this memory region.
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Mem\+Advice\+Unset\+Read\+Mostly\+:} Undoes the effect of \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Mem\+Advice\+Read\+Mostly} and also prevents the Unified Memory driver from attempting heuristic read-\/duplication on the memory range. Any read-\/duplicated copies of the data will be collapsed into a single copy. The location for the collapsed copy will be the preferred location if the page has a preferred location and one of the read-\/duplicated copies was resident at that location. Otherwise, the location chosen is arbitrary.
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Mem\+Advise\+Set\+Preferred\+Location\+:} This advice sets the preferred location for the data to be the memory belonging to {\ttfamily device}. Passing in cuda\+Cpu\+Device\+Id for {\ttfamily device} sets the preferred location as host memory. If {\ttfamily device} is a GPU, then it must have a non-\/zero value for the device attribute cuda\+Dev\+Attr\+Concurrent\+Managed\+Access. Setting the preferred location does not cause data to migrate to that location immediately. Instead, it guides the migration policy when a fault occurs on that memory region. If the data is already in its preferred location and the faulting processor can establish a mapping without requiring the data to be migrated, then data migration will be avoided. On the other hand, if the data is not in its preferred location or if a direct mapping cannot be established, then it will be migrated to the processor accessing it. It is important to note that setting the preferred location does not prevent data prefetching done using \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga4a666ced2163d18849c59c608bfbd208}{cuda\+Mem\+Prefetch\+Async}. Having a preferred location can override the page thrash detection and resolution logic in the Unified Memory driver. Normally, if a page is detected to be constantly thrashing between for example host and device memory, the page may eventually be pinned to host memory by the Unified Memory driver. But if the preferred location is set as device memory, then the page will continue to thrash indefinitely. If cuda\+Mem\+Advise\+Set\+Read\+Mostly is also set on this memory region or any subset of it, then the policies associated with that advice will override the policies of this advice, unless read accesses from {\ttfamily device} will not result in a read-\/only copy being created on that device as outlined in description for the advice cuda\+Mem\+Advise\+Set\+Read\+Mostly. If the memory region refers to valid system-\/allocated pageable memory, then {\ttfamily device} must have a non-\/zero value for the device attribute cuda\+Dev\+Attr\+Pageable\+Memory\+Access. Additionally, if {\ttfamily device} has a non-\/zero value for the device attribute cuda\+Dev\+Attr\+Pageable\+Memory\+Access\+Uses\+Host\+Page\+Tables, then this call has no effect. Note however that this behavior may change in the future.
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Mem\+Advise\+Unset\+Preferred\+Location\+:} Undoes the effect of cuda\+Mem\+Advise\+Set\+Preferred\+Location and changes the preferred location to none.
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Mem\+Advise\+Set\+Accessed\+By\+:} This advice implies that the data will be accessed by {\ttfamily device}. Passing in \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gab3de5e703b559507c39a6a02127e2967}{cuda\+Cpu\+Device\+Id} for {\ttfamily device} will set the advice for the CPU. If {\ttfamily device} is a GPU, then the device attribute cuda\+Dev\+Attr\+Concurrent\+Managed\+Access must be non-\/zero. This advice does not cause data migration and has no impact on the location of the data per se. Instead, it causes the data to always be mapped in the specified processor\textquotesingle{}s page tables, as long as the location of the data permits a mapping to be established. If the data gets migrated for any reason, the mappings are updated accordingly. This advice is recommended in scenarios where data locality is not important, but avoiding faults is. Consider for example a system containing multiple GPUs with peer-\/to-\/peer access enabled, where the data located on one GPU is occasionally accessed by peer GPUs. In such scenarios, migrating data over to the other GPUs is not as important because the accesses are infrequent and the overhead of migration may be too high. But preventing faults can still help improve performance, and so having a mapping set up in advance is useful. Note that on CPU access of this data, the data may be migrated to host memory because the CPU typically cannot access device memory directly. Any GPU that had the \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Mem\+Advice\+Set\+Accessed\+By} flag set for this data will now have its mapping updated to point to the page in host memory. If cuda\+Mem\+Advise\+Set\+Read\+Mostly is also set on this memory region or any subset of it, then the policies associated with that advice will override the policies of this advice. Additionally, if the preferred location of this memory region or any subset of it is also {\ttfamily device}, then the policies associated with cuda\+Mem\+Advise\+Set\+Preferred\+Location will override the policies of this advice. If the memory region refers to valid system-\/allocated pageable memory, then {\ttfamily device} must have a non-\/zero value for the device attribute cuda\+Dev\+Attr\+Pageable\+Memory\+Access. Additionally, if {\ttfamily device} has a non-\/zero value for the device attribute cuda\+Dev\+Attr\+Pageable\+Memory\+Access\+Uses\+Host\+Page\+Tables, then this call has no effect.
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Mem\+Advise\+Unset\+Accessed\+By\+:} Undoes the effect of cuda\+Mem\+Advise\+Set\+Accessed\+By. Any mappings to the data from {\ttfamily device} may be removed at any time causing accesses to result in non-\/fatal page faults. If the memory region refers to valid system-\/allocated pageable memory, then {\ttfamily device} must have a non-\/zero value for the device attribute cuda\+Dev\+Attr\+Pageable\+Memory\+Access. Additionally, if {\ttfamily device} has a non-\/zero value for the device attribute cuda\+Dev\+Attr\+Pageable\+Memory\+Access\+Uses\+Host\+Page\+Tables, then this call has no effect.
\end{DoxyItemize}

{\em count} & -\/ Size in bytes of the memory range \\
\hline
{\em advice} & -\/ Advice to be applied for the specified memory range \\
\hline
{\em device} & -\/ Device to apply the advice for\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\end{DoxyReturn}

\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaMemcpy()}{cudaMemcpy()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Memcpy (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{dst,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{src,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{count,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{enum}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga8ce1ad49a1e77a595edcb25ac795cd0f}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Kind}}}]{kind }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Copies data between host and device. 

Copies {\ttfamily count} bytes from the memory area pointed to by {\ttfamily src} to the memory area pointed to by {\ttfamily dst}, where {\ttfamily kind} specifies the direction of the copy, and must be one of cuda\+Memcpy\+Host\+To\+Host, cuda\+Memcpy\+Host\+To\+Device, cuda\+Memcpy\+Device\+To\+Host, cuda\+Memcpy\+Device\+To\+Device, or \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Default}. Passing \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Default} is recommended, in which case the type of transfer is inferred from the pointer values. However, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Default} is only allowed on systems that support unified virtual addressing. Calling \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gae2bbb87e03bde890140dae4b348e1886}{cuda\+Memcpy()} with dst and src pointers that do not match the direction of the copy results in an undefined behavior.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em dst} & -\/ Destination memory address \\
\hline
{\em src} & -\/ Source memory address \\
\hline
{\em count} & -\/ Size in bytes to copy \\
\hline
{\em kind} & -\/ Type of transfer\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
cuda\+Success, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Memcpy\+Direction \textbackslash{}notefnerr \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+init\+\_\+rt \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+callback
\end{DoxyReturn}
\textbackslash{}note\+\_\+sync \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+memcpy

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaMemcpy2D()}{cudaMemcpy2D()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Memcpy2D (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{dst,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{dpitch,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{src,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{spitch,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{width,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{height,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{enum}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga8ce1ad49a1e77a595edcb25ac795cd0f}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Kind}}}]{kind }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Copies data between host and device. 

Copies a matrix ({\ttfamily height} rows of {\ttfamily width} bytes each) from the memory area pointed to by {\ttfamily src} to the memory area pointed to by {\ttfamily dst}, where {\ttfamily kind} specifies the direction of the copy, and must be one of cuda\+Memcpy\+Host\+To\+Host, cuda\+Memcpy\+Host\+To\+Device, cuda\+Memcpy\+Device\+To\+Host, cuda\+Memcpy\+Device\+To\+Device, or \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Default}. Passing \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Default} is recommended, in which case the type of transfer is inferred from the pointer values. However, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Default} is only allowed on systems that support unified virtual addressing. {\ttfamily dpitch} and {\ttfamily spitch} are the widths in memory in bytes of the 2D arrays pointed to by {\ttfamily dst} and {\ttfamily src}, including any padding added to the end of each row. The memory areas may not overlap. {\ttfamily width} must not exceed either {\ttfamily dpitch} or {\ttfamily spitch}. Calling \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gadf7361e67d7228dbb554f1ccb47d54b1}{cuda\+Memcpy2\+D()} with {\ttfamily dst} and {\ttfamily src} pointers that do not match the direction of the copy results in an undefined behavior. \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gadf7361e67d7228dbb554f1ccb47d54b1}{cuda\+Memcpy2\+D()} returns an error if {\ttfamily dpitch} or {\ttfamily spitch} exceeds the maximum allowed.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em dst} & -\/ Destination memory address \\
\hline
{\em dpitch} & -\/ Pitch of destination memory \\
\hline
{\em src} & -\/ Source memory address \\
\hline
{\em spitch} & -\/ Pitch of source memory \\
\hline
{\em width} & -\/ Width of matrix transfer (columns in bytes) \\
\hline
{\em height} & -\/ Height of matrix transfer (rows) \\
\hline
{\em kind} & -\/ Type of transfer\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{cudaMemcpy2DArrayToArray@{cudaMemcpy2DArrayToArray}!Memory Management@{Memory Management}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaMemcpy2DArrayToArray()}{cudaMemcpy2DArrayToArray()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Memcpy2\+DArray\+To\+Array (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gaaf8b3ba752727d996074a71ee997ce68}{cuda\+Array\+\_\+t}}}]{dst,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{w\+Offset\+Dst,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{h\+Offset\+Dst,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga9a3dce149702581dbc3fc2fb9bb813b0}{cuda\+Array\+\_\+const\+\_\+t}}}]{src,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{w\+Offset\+Src,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{h\+Offset\+Src,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{width,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{height,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{enum}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga8ce1ad49a1e77a595edcb25ac795cd0f}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Kind}} kind }]{\+\_\+\+\_\+dvcuda\+Memcpy\+Device\+To\+Device }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Copies data between host and device. 

Copies a matrix ({\ttfamily height} rows of {\ttfamily width} bytes each) from the CUDA array {\ttfamily src} starting at {\ttfamily h\+Offset\+Src} rows and {\ttfamily w\+Offset\+Src} bytes from the upper left corner to the CUDA array {\ttfamily dst} starting at {\ttfamily h\+Offset\+Dst} rows and {\ttfamily w\+Offset\+Dst} bytes from the upper left corner, where {\ttfamily kind} specifies the direction of the copy, and must be one of cuda\+Memcpy\+Host\+To\+Host, cuda\+Memcpy\+Host\+To\+Device, cuda\+Memcpy\+Device\+To\+Host, cuda\+Memcpy\+Device\+To\+Device, or \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Default}. Passing \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Default} is recommended, in which case the type of transfer is inferred from the pointer values. However, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Default} is only allowed on systems that support unified virtual addressing. {\ttfamily w\+Offset\+Dst} + {\ttfamily width} must not exceed the width of the CUDA array {\ttfamily dst}. {\ttfamily w\+Offset\+Src} + {\ttfamily width} must not exceed the width of the CUDA array {\ttfamily src}.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}

{\em w\+Offset\+Dst} & -\/ Destination starting X offset (columns in bytes) \\
\hline
{\em h\+Offset\+Dst} & -\/ Destination starting Y offset (rows) \\
\hline
{\em src} & -\/ Source memory address \\
\hline
{\em w\+Offset\+Src} & -\/ Source starting X offset (columns in bytes) \\
\hline
{\em h\+Offset\+Src} & -\/ Source starting Y offset (rows) \\
\hline
{\em width} & -\/ Width of matrix transfer (columns in bytes) \\
\hline
{\em height} & -\/ Height of matrix transfer (rows) \\
\hline
{\em kind} & -\/ Type of transfer\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

cuda\+Success, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Memcpy\+Direction \textbackslash{}notefnerr \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+sync \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+init\+\_\+rt \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+callback
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{cudaMemcpy2DAsync@{cudaMemcpy2DAsync}!Memory Management@{Memory Management}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaMemcpy2DAsync()}{cudaMemcpy2DAsync()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+cudart\+\_\+builtin\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Memcpy2\+DAsync (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{dst,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{dpitch,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{src,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{spitch,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{width,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{height,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{enum}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga8ce1ad49a1e77a595edcb25ac795cd0f}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Kind}}}]{kind,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gae6a6dd5bf3109046a07da4b735234e81}{cuda\+Stream\+\_\+t}} stream }]{\+\_\+\+\_\+dv0 }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Copies data between host and device. 

Copies a matrix ({\ttfamily height} rows of {\ttfamily width} bytes each) from the memory area pointed to by {\ttfamily src} to the memory area pointed to by {\ttfamily dst}, where {\ttfamily kind} specifies the direction of the copy, and must be one of cuda\+Memcpy\+Host\+To\+Host, cuda\+Memcpy\+Host\+To\+Device, cuda\+Memcpy\+Device\+To\+Host, cuda\+Memcpy\+Device\+To\+Device, or \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Default}. Passing \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Default} is recommended, in which case the type of transfer is inferred from the pointer values. However, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Default} is only allowed on systems that support unified virtual addressing. {\ttfamily dpitch} and {\ttfamily spitch} are the widths in memory in bytes of the 2D arrays pointed to by {\ttfamily dst} and {\ttfamily src}, including any padding added to the end of each row. The memory areas may not overlap. {\ttfamily width} must not exceed either {\ttfamily dpitch} or {\ttfamily spitch}.

Calling \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga18f73e4d8f45009a3a733407b0ab5fbf}{cuda\+Memcpy2\+DAsync()} with {\ttfamily dst} and {\ttfamily src} pointers that do not match the direction of the copy results in an undefined behavior. \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga18f73e4d8f45009a3a733407b0ab5fbf}{cuda\+Memcpy2\+DAsync()} returns an error if {\ttfamily dpitch} or {\ttfamily spitch} is greater than the maximum allowed.

\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga18f73e4d8f45009a3a733407b0ab5fbf}{cuda\+Memcpy2\+DAsync()} is asynchronous with respect to the host, so the call may return before the copy is complete. The copy can optionally be associated to a stream by passing a non-\/zero {\ttfamily stream} argument. If {\ttfamily kind} is cuda\+Memcpy\+Host\+To\+Device or cuda\+Memcpy\+Device\+To\+Host and {\ttfamily stream} is non-\/zero, the copy may overlap with operations in other streams.

The device version of this function only handles device to device copies and cannot be given local or shared pointers.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em dst} & -\/ Destination memory address \\
\hline
{\em dpitch} & -\/ Pitch of destination memory \\
\hline
{\em src} & -\/ Source memory address \\
\hline
{\em spitch} & -\/ Pitch of source memory \\
\hline
{\em width} & -\/ Width of matrix transfer (columns in bytes) \\
\hline
{\em height} & -\/ Height of matrix transfer (rows) \\
\hline
{\em kind} & -\/ Type of transfer \\
\hline
{\em stream} & -\/ Stream identifier\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
cuda\+Success, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Pitch\+Value, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Memcpy\+Direction \textbackslash{}notefnerr \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+async \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+null\+\_\+stream \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+init\+\_\+rt \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+callback \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+memcpy
\end{DoxyReturn}

\end{DoxySeeAlso}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Memcpy2\+DFrom\+Array (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{dst,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{dpitch,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga9a3dce149702581dbc3fc2fb9bb813b0}{cuda\+Array\+\_\+const\+\_\+t}}}]{src,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{w\+Offset,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{h\+Offset,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{width,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{height,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{enum}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga8ce1ad49a1e77a595edcb25ac795cd0f}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Kind}}}]{kind }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Copies data between host and device. 

Copies a matrix ({\ttfamily height} rows of {\ttfamily width} bytes each) from the CUDA array {\ttfamily src} starting at {\ttfamily h\+Offset} rows and {\ttfamily w\+Offset} bytes from the upper left corner to the memory area pointed to by {\ttfamily dst}, where {\ttfamily kind} specifies the direction of the copy, and must be one of cuda\+Memcpy\+Host\+To\+Host, cuda\+Memcpy\+Host\+To\+Device, cuda\+Memcpy\+Device\+To\+Host, cuda\+Memcpy\+Device\+To\+Device, or \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Default}. Passing \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Default} is recommended, in which case the type of transfer is inferred from the pointer values. However, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Default} is only allowed on systems that support unified virtual addressing. {\ttfamily dpitch} is the width in memory in bytes of the 2D array pointed to by {\ttfamily dst}, including any padding added to the end of each row. {\ttfamily w\+Offset} + {\ttfamily width} must not exceed the width of the CUDA array {\ttfamily src}. {\ttfamily width} must not exceed {\ttfamily dpitch}. \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga94a63ef65830ce0c5a8bc8b8208caacb}{cuda\+Memcpy2\+DFrom\+Array()} returns an error if {\ttfamily dpitch} exceeds the maximum allowed.

\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gae2bbb87e03bde890140dae4b348e1886}{cuda\+Memcpy}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gadf7361e67d7228dbb554f1ccb47d54b1}{cuda\+Memcpy2D}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga6ea4e52dd6157f45425fdcff3f6d9d3d}{cuda\+Memcpy2\+DTo\+Array}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gac8f08a316c1b641bb7ecc85012ddf25d}{cuda\+Memcpy2\+DArray\+To\+Array}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gab81cd4dead648a67aa745cb1e10059ba}{cuda\+Memcpy\+To\+Symbol}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga9356cb69eef5a12c7ea255c1b010f121}{cuda\+Memcpy\+From\+Symbol}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gafb6d05d580838d8efbe581ca69cd7ac7}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Async}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga18f73e4d8f45009a3a733407b0ab5fbf}{cuda\+Memcpy2\+DAsync}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga5e33c77f7fe3cbc1add4671604c30b7d}{cuda\+Memcpy2\+DTo\+Array\+Async}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gae66d22de38a11ce8e09f8f788b2cf275}{cuda\+Memcpy2\+DFrom\+Array\+Async}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga6110c29da79fc76851d202e27de9aa2c}{cuda\+Memcpy\+To\+Symbol\+Async}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga4be8411d879e1ed4589da65c87d99857}{cuda\+Memcpy\+From\+Symbol\+Async}, cu\+Memcpy2D, cu\+Memcpy2\+DUnaligned

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaMemcpy2DFromArrayAsync()}{cudaMemcpy2DFromArrayAsync()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Memcpy2\+DFrom\+Array\+Async (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{dst,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{dpitch,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga9a3dce149702581dbc3fc2fb9bb813b0}{cuda\+Array\+\_\+const\+\_\+t}}}]{src,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{w\+Offset,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{h\+Offset,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{width,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{height,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{enum}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga8ce1ad49a1e77a595edcb25ac795cd0f}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Kind}}}]{kind,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gae6a6dd5bf3109046a07da4b735234e81}{cuda\+Stream\+\_\+t}} stream }]{\+\_\+\+\_\+dv0 }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Copies data between host and device. 

Copies a matrix ({\ttfamily height} rows of {\ttfamily width} bytes each) from the CUDA array {\ttfamily src} starting at {\ttfamily h\+Offset} rows and {\ttfamily w\+Offset} bytes from the upper left corner to the memory area pointed to by {\ttfamily dst}, where {\ttfamily kind} specifies the direction of the copy, and must be one of cuda\+Memcpy\+Host\+To\+Host, cuda\+Memcpy\+Host\+To\+Device, cuda\+Memcpy\+Device\+To\+Host, cuda\+Memcpy\+Device\+To\+Device, or \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Default}. Passing \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Default} is recommended, in which case the type of transfer is inferred from the pointer values. However, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Default} is only allowed on systems that support unified virtual addressing. {\ttfamily dpitch} is the width in memory in bytes of the 2D array pointed to by {\ttfamily dst}, including any padding added to the end of each row. {\ttfamily w\+Offset} + {\ttfamily width} must not exceed the width of the CUDA array {\ttfamily src}. {\ttfamily width} must not exceed {\ttfamily dpitch}. \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gae66d22de38a11ce8e09f8f788b2cf275}{cuda\+Memcpy2\+DFrom\+Array\+Async()} returns an error if {\ttfamily dpitch} exceeds the maximum allowed.

\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gae66d22de38a11ce8e09f8f788b2cf275}{cuda\+Memcpy2\+DFrom\+Array\+Async()} is asynchronous with respect to the host, so the call may return before the copy is complete. The copy can optionally be associated to a stream by passing a non-\/zero {\ttfamily stream} argument. If {\ttfamily kind} is cuda\+Memcpy\+Host\+To\+Device or cuda\+Memcpy\+Device\+To\+Host and {\ttfamily stream} is non-\/zero, the copy may overlap with operations in other streams.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em dst} & -\/ Destination memory address \\
\hline
{\em dpitch} & -\/ Pitch of destination memory \\
\hline
{\em src} & -\/ Source memory address \\
\hline
{\em w\+Offset} & -\/ Source starting X offset (columns in bytes) \\
\hline
{\em h\+Offset} & -\/ Source starting Y offset (rows) \\
\hline
{\em width} & -\/ Width of matrix transfer (columns in bytes) \\
\hline
{\em height} & -\/ Height of matrix transfer (rows) \\
\hline
{\em kind} & -\/ Type of transfer \\
\hline
{\em stream} & -\/ Stream identifier\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
cuda\+Success, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Pitch\+Value, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Memcpy\+Direction \textbackslash{}notefnerr \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+async \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+null\+\_\+stream \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+init\+\_\+rt \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+callback \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+memcpy
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Memcpy2\+DTo\+Array (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gaaf8b3ba752727d996074a71ee997ce68}{cuda\+Array\+\_\+t}}}]{dst,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{w\+Offset,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{h\+Offset,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{src,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{spitch,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{width,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{height,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{enum}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga8ce1ad49a1e77a595edcb25ac795cd0f}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Kind}}}]{kind }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Copies data between host and device. 

Copies a matrix ({\ttfamily height} rows of {\ttfamily width} bytes each) from the memory area pointed to by {\ttfamily src} to the CUDA array {\ttfamily dst} starting at {\ttfamily h\+Offset} rows and {\ttfamily w\+Offset} bytes from the upper left corner, where {\ttfamily kind} specifies the direction of the copy, and must be one of cuda\+Memcpy\+Host\+To\+Host, cuda\+Memcpy\+Host\+To\+Device, cuda\+Memcpy\+Device\+To\+Host, cuda\+Memcpy\+Device\+To\+Device, or \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Default}. Passing \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Default} is recommended, in which case the type of transfer is inferred from the pointer values. However, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Default} is only allowed on systems that support unified virtual addressing. {\ttfamily spitch} is the width in memory in bytes of the 2D array pointed to by {\ttfamily src}, including any padding added to the end of each row. {\ttfamily w\+Offset} + {\ttfamily width} must not exceed the width of the CUDA array {\ttfamily dst}. {\ttfamily width} must not exceed {\ttfamily spitch}. \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga6ea4e52dd6157f45425fdcff3f6d9d3d}{cuda\+Memcpy2\+DTo\+Array()} returns an error if {\ttfamily spitch} exceeds the maximum allowed.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaMemcpy2DToArrayAsync()}{cudaMemcpy2DToArrayAsync()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Memcpy2\+DTo\+Array\+Async (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gaaf8b3ba752727d996074a71ee997ce68}{cuda\+Array\+\_\+t}}}]{dst,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{w\+Offset,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{h\+Offset,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{src,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{spitch,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{width,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{height,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{enum}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga8ce1ad49a1e77a595edcb25ac795cd0f}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Kind}}}]{kind,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gae6a6dd5bf3109046a07da4b735234e81}{cuda\+Stream\+\_\+t}} stream }]{\+\_\+\+\_\+dv0 }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Copies data between host and device. 

Copies a matrix ({\ttfamily height} rows of {\ttfamily width} bytes each) from the memory area pointed to by {\ttfamily src} to the CUDA array {\ttfamily dst} starting at {\ttfamily h\+Offset} rows and {\ttfamily w\+Offset} bytes from the upper left corner, where {\ttfamily kind} specifies the direction of the copy, and must be one of cuda\+Memcpy\+Host\+To\+Host, cuda\+Memcpy\+Host\+To\+Device, cuda\+Memcpy\+Device\+To\+Host, cuda\+Memcpy\+Device\+To\+Device, or \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Default}. Passing \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Default} is recommended, in which case the type of transfer is inferred from the pointer values. However, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Default} is only allowed on systems that support unified virtual addressing. {\ttfamily spitch} is the width in memory in bytes of the 2D array pointed to by {\ttfamily src}, including any padding added to the end of each row. {\ttfamily w\+Offset} + {\ttfamily width} must not exceed the width of the CUDA array {\ttfamily dst}. {\ttfamily width} must not exceed {\ttfamily spitch}. \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga5e33c77f7fe3cbc1add4671604c30b7d}{cuda\+Memcpy2\+DTo\+Array\+Async()} returns an error if {\ttfamily spitch} exceeds the maximum allowed.

\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga5e33c77f7fe3cbc1add4671604c30b7d}{cuda\+Memcpy2\+DTo\+Array\+Async()} is asynchronous with respect to the host, so the call may return before the copy is complete. The copy can optionally be associated to a stream by passing a non-\/zero {\ttfamily stream} argument. If {\ttfamily kind} is cuda\+Memcpy\+Host\+To\+Device or cuda\+Memcpy\+Device\+To\+Host and {\ttfamily stream} is non-\/zero, the copy may overlap with operations in other streams.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Memcpy3D (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{struct}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structcuda_memcpy3_d_parms}{cuda\+Memcpy3\+DParms}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Copies data between 3D objects.

\end{DoxyCode}


\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga60a55856b9b01a0620ca1c657debed53}{cuda\+Memcpy3\+D()} copies data betwen two 3D objects. The source and destination objects may be in either host memory, device memory, or a CUDA array. The source, destination, extent, and kind of copy performed is specified by the \doxylink{structcuda_memcpy3_d_parms}{cuda\+Memcpy3\+DParms} struct which should be initialized to zero before use\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{structcuda_memcpy3_d_parms}{cudaMemcpy3DParms}}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{myParms}}\ =\ \{0\};}

\end{DoxyCode}


The struct passed to \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga60a55856b9b01a0620ca1c657debed53}{cuda\+Memcpy3\+D()} must specify one of {\ttfamily src\+Array} or {\ttfamily src\+Ptr} and one of {\ttfamily dst\+Array} or {\ttfamily dst\+Ptr}. Passing more than one non-\/zero source or destination will cause \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga60a55856b9b01a0620ca1c657debed53}{cuda\+Memcpy3\+D()} to return an error.

The {\ttfamily src\+Pos} and {\ttfamily dst\+Pos} fields are optional offsets into the source and destination objects and are defined in units of each object\textquotesingle{}s elements. The element for a host or device pointer is assumed to be {\bfseries{unsigned char}}.

The {\ttfamily extent} field defines the dimensions of the transferred area in elements. If a CUDA array is participating in the copy, the extent is defined in terms of that array\textquotesingle{}s elements. If no CUDA array is participating in the copy then the extents are defined in elements of {\bfseries{unsigned char}}.

The {\ttfamily kind} field defines the direction of the copy. It must be one of cuda\+Memcpy\+Host\+To\+Host, cuda\+Memcpy\+Host\+To\+Device, cuda\+Memcpy\+Device\+To\+Host, cuda\+Memcpy\+Device\+To\+Device, or \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Default}. Passing \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Default} is recommended, in which case the type of transfer is inferred from the pointer values. However, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Default} is only allowed on systems that support unified virtual addressing. For cuda\+Memcpy\+Host\+To\+Host or cuda\+Memcpy\+Host\+To\+Device or cuda\+Memcpy\+Device\+To\+Host passed as kind and cuda\+Array type passed as source or destination, if the kind implies cuda\+Array type to be present on the host, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga60a55856b9b01a0620ca1c657debed53}{cuda\+Memcpy3\+D()} will disregard that implication and silently correct the kind based on the fact that cuda\+Array type can only be present on the device.

If the source and destination are both arrays, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga60a55856b9b01a0620ca1c657debed53}{cuda\+Memcpy3\+D()} will return an error if they do not have the same element size.

The source and destination object may not overlap. If overlapping source and destination objects are specified, undefined behavior will result.

The source object must entirely contain the region defined by {\ttfamily src\+Pos} and {\ttfamily extent}. The destination object must entirely contain the region defined by {\ttfamily dst\+Pos} and {\ttfamily extent}.

\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga60a55856b9b01a0620ca1c657debed53}{cuda\+Memcpy3\+D()} returns an error if the pitch of {\ttfamily src\+Ptr} or {\ttfamily dst\+Ptr} exceeds the maximum allowed. The pitch of a \doxylink{structcuda_pitched_ptr}{cuda\+Pitched\+Ptr} allocated with \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga38d900061e670e541cebf5042e0e7739}{cuda\+Malloc3\+D()} will always be valid.

{\em p} & -\/ 3D memory copy parameters\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
cuda\+Success, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Pitch\+Value, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Memcpy\+Direction \textbackslash{}notefnerr \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+sync \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+init\+\_\+rt \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+callback
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga38d900061e670e541cebf5042e0e7739}{cuda\+Malloc3D}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gaf3a3790459bdc37339fff10927ef8214}{cuda\+Malloc3\+DArray}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga2c9bdd7406ea3a1215ca4f2bf9e3681f}{cuda\+Memset3D}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga703efb5f7d7223709d00e1ce295e8bb8}{cuda\+Memcpy3\+DAsync}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gae2bbb87e03bde890140dae4b348e1886}{cuda\+Memcpy}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gadf7361e67d7228dbb554f1ccb47d54b1}{cuda\+Memcpy2D}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga6ea4e52dd6157f45425fdcff3f6d9d3d}{cuda\+Memcpy2\+DTo\+Array}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga94a63ef65830ce0c5a8bc8b8208caacb}{cuda\+Memcpy2\+DFrom\+Array}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gac8f08a316c1b641bb7ecc85012ddf25d}{cuda\+Memcpy2\+DArray\+To\+Array}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gab81cd4dead648a67aa745cb1e10059ba}{cuda\+Memcpy\+To\+Symbol}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga9356cb69eef5a12c7ea255c1b010f121}{cuda\+Memcpy\+From\+Symbol}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gafb6d05d580838d8efbe581ca69cd7ac7}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Async}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga18f73e4d8f45009a3a733407b0ab5fbf}{cuda\+Memcpy2\+DAsync}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga5e33c77f7fe3cbc1add4671604c30b7d}{cuda\+Memcpy2\+DTo\+Array\+Async}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gae66d22de38a11ce8e09f8f788b2cf275}{cuda\+Memcpy2\+DFrom\+Array\+Async}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga6110c29da79fc76851d202e27de9aa2c}{cuda\+Memcpy\+To\+Symbol\+Async}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga4be8411d879e1ed4589da65c87d99857}{cuda\+Memcpy\+From\+Symbol\+Async}, make\+\_\+cuda\+Extent, make\+\_\+cuda\+Pos, cu\+Memcpy3D

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+cudart\+\_\+builtin\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Memcpy3\+DAsync (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{struct}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structcuda_memcpy3_d_parms}{cuda\+Memcpy3\+DParms}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gae6a6dd5bf3109046a07da4b735234e81}{cuda\+Stream\+\_\+t}} stream }]{\+\_\+\+\_\+dv0 }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Copies data between 3D objects.

\end{DoxyCode}


\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga703efb5f7d7223709d00e1ce295e8bb8}{cuda\+Memcpy3\+DAsync()} copies data betwen two 3D objects. The source and destination objects may be in either host memory, device memory, or a CUDA array. The source, destination, extent, and kind of copy performed is specified by the \doxylink{structcuda_memcpy3_d_parms}{cuda\+Memcpy3\+DParms} struct which should be initialized to zero before use\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{structcuda_memcpy3_d_parms}{cudaMemcpy3DParms}}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{myParms}}\ =\ \{0\};}

\end{DoxyCode}


The struct passed to \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga703efb5f7d7223709d00e1ce295e8bb8}{cuda\+Memcpy3\+DAsync()} must specify one of {\ttfamily src\+Array} or {\ttfamily src\+Ptr} and one of {\ttfamily dst\+Array} or {\ttfamily dst\+Ptr}. Passing more than one non-\/zero source or destination will cause \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga703efb5f7d7223709d00e1ce295e8bb8}{cuda\+Memcpy3\+DAsync()} to return an error.

The {\ttfamily src\+Pos} and {\ttfamily dst\+Pos} fields are optional offsets into the source and destination objects and are defined in units of each object\textquotesingle{}s elements. The element for a host or device pointer is assumed to be {\bfseries{unsigned char}}. For CUDA arrays, positions must be in the range \mbox{[}0, 2048) for any dimension.

The {\ttfamily extent} field defines the dimensions of the transferred area in elements. If a CUDA array is participating in the copy, the extent is defined in terms of that array\textquotesingle{}s elements. If no CUDA array is participating in the copy then the extents are defined in elements of {\bfseries{unsigned char}}.

The {\ttfamily kind} field defines the direction of the copy. It must be one of cuda\+Memcpy\+Host\+To\+Host, cuda\+Memcpy\+Host\+To\+Device, cuda\+Memcpy\+Device\+To\+Host, cuda\+Memcpy\+Device\+To\+Device, or \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Default}. Passing \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Default} is recommended, in which case the type of transfer is inferred from the pointer values. However, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Default} is only allowed on systems that support unified virtual addressing. For cuda\+Memcpy\+Host\+To\+Host or cuda\+Memcpy\+Host\+To\+Device or cuda\+Memcpy\+Device\+To\+Host passed as kind and cuda\+Array type passed as source or destination, if the kind implies cuda\+Array type to be present on the host, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga703efb5f7d7223709d00e1ce295e8bb8}{cuda\+Memcpy3\+DAsync()} will disregard that implication and silently correct the kind based on the fact that cuda\+Array type can only be present on the device.

If the source and destination are both arrays, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga703efb5f7d7223709d00e1ce295e8bb8}{cuda\+Memcpy3\+DAsync()} will return an error if they do not have the same element size.

The source and destination object may not overlap. If overlapping source and destination objects are specified, undefined behavior will result.

The source object must lie entirely within the region defined by {\ttfamily src\+Pos} and {\ttfamily extent}. The destination object must lie entirely within the region defined by {\ttfamily dst\+Pos} and {\ttfamily extent}.

\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga703efb5f7d7223709d00e1ce295e8bb8}{cuda\+Memcpy3\+DAsync()} returns an error if the pitch of {\ttfamily src\+Ptr} or {\ttfamily dst\+Ptr} exceeds the maximum allowed. The pitch of a \doxylink{structcuda_pitched_ptr}{cuda\+Pitched\+Ptr} allocated with \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga38d900061e670e541cebf5042e0e7739}{cuda\+Malloc3\+D()} will always be valid.

\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga703efb5f7d7223709d00e1ce295e8bb8}{cuda\+Memcpy3\+DAsync()} is asynchronous with respect to the host, so the call may return before the copy is complete. The copy can optionally be associated to a stream by passing a non-\/zero {\ttfamily stream} argument. If {\ttfamily kind} is cuda\+Memcpy\+Host\+To\+Device or cuda\+Memcpy\+Device\+To\+Host and {\ttfamily stream} is non-\/zero, the copy may overlap with operations in other streams.

The device version of this function only handles device to device copies and cannot be given local or shared pointers.

\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga38d900061e670e541cebf5042e0e7739}{cuda\+Malloc3D}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gaf3a3790459bdc37339fff10927ef8214}{cuda\+Malloc3\+DArray}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga2c9bdd7406ea3a1215ca4f2bf9e3681f}{cuda\+Memset3D}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga60a55856b9b01a0620ca1c657debed53}{cuda\+Memcpy3D}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gae2bbb87e03bde890140dae4b348e1886}{cuda\+Memcpy}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gadf7361e67d7228dbb554f1ccb47d54b1}{cuda\+Memcpy2D}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga6ea4e52dd6157f45425fdcff3f6d9d3d}{cuda\+Memcpy2\+DTo\+Array}, \+::\+:\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga94a63ef65830ce0c5a8bc8b8208caacb}{cuda\+Memcpy2\+DFrom\+Array}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gac8f08a316c1b641bb7ecc85012ddf25d}{cuda\+Memcpy2\+DArray\+To\+Array}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gab81cd4dead648a67aa745cb1e10059ba}{cuda\+Memcpy\+To\+Symbol}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga9356cb69eef5a12c7ea255c1b010f121}{cuda\+Memcpy\+From\+Symbol}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gafb6d05d580838d8efbe581ca69cd7ac7}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Async}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga18f73e4d8f45009a3a733407b0ab5fbf}{cuda\+Memcpy2\+DAsync}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga5e33c77f7fe3cbc1add4671604c30b7d}{cuda\+Memcpy2\+DTo\+Array\+Async}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gae66d22de38a11ce8e09f8f788b2cf275}{cuda\+Memcpy2\+DFrom\+Array\+Async}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga6110c29da79fc76851d202e27de9aa2c}{cuda\+Memcpy\+To\+Symbol\+Async}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga4be8411d879e1ed4589da65c87d99857}{cuda\+Memcpy\+From\+Symbol\+Async}, make\+\_\+cuda\+Extent, make\+\_\+cuda\+Pos, cu\+Memcpy3\+DAsync 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga3b1866dc30a2af88914742a2fe2bc9b1}\label{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga3b1866dc30a2af88914742a2fe2bc9b1} 
\index{Memory Management@{Memory Management}!cudaMemcpy3DPeer@{cudaMemcpy3DPeer}}
\index{cudaMemcpy3DPeer@{cudaMemcpy3DPeer}!Memory Management@{Memory Management}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaMemcpy3DPeer()}{cudaMemcpy3DPeer()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Memcpy3\+DPeer (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{struct}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structcuda_memcpy3_d_peer_parms}{cuda\+Memcpy3\+DPeer\+Parms}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Copies memory between devices. 

Perform a 3D memory copy according to the parameters specified in {\ttfamily p}. See the definition of the \doxylink{structcuda_memcpy3_d_peer_parms}{cuda\+Memcpy3\+DPeer\+Parms} structure for documentation of its parameters.

Note that this function is synchronous with respect to the host only if the source or destination of the transfer is host memory. Note also that this copy is serialized with respect to all pending and future asynchronous work in to the current device, the copy\textquotesingle{}s source device, and the copy\textquotesingle{}s destination device (use \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga5fbe9d79a247ae6de5729c9e78721241}{cuda\+Memcpy3\+DPeer\+Async} to avoid this synchronization).


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em p} & -\/ Parameters for the memory copy\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
cuda\+Success, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Device \textbackslash{}notefnerr \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+sync \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+init\+\_\+rt \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+callback
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaMemcpy3DPeerAsync()}{cudaMemcpy3DPeerAsync()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Memcpy3\+DPeer\+Async (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{struct}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structcuda_memcpy3_d_peer_parms}{cuda\+Memcpy3\+DPeer\+Parms}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gae6a6dd5bf3109046a07da4b735234e81}{cuda\+Stream\+\_\+t}} stream }]{\+\_\+\+\_\+dv0 }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Copies memory between devices asynchronously. 

Perform a 3D memory copy according to the parameters specified in {\ttfamily p}. See the definition of the \doxylink{structcuda_memcpy3_d_peer_parms}{cuda\+Memcpy3\+DPeer\+Parms} structure for documentation of its parameters.
