\index{Memory Management@{Memory Management}!cudaMemcpyAsync@{cudaMemcpyAsync}}
\index{cudaMemcpyAsync@{cudaMemcpyAsync}!Memory Management@{Memory Management}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaMemcpyAsync()}{cudaMemcpyAsync()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+cudart\+\_\+builtin\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Memcpy\+Async (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{dst,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{src,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{count,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{enum}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga8ce1ad49a1e77a595edcb25ac795cd0f}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Kind}}}]{kind,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gae6a6dd5bf3109046a07da4b735234e81}{cuda\+Stream\+\_\+t}} stream }]{\+\_\+\+\_\+dv0 }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Copies data between host and device. 

Copies {\ttfamily count} bytes from the memory area pointed to by {\ttfamily src} to the memory area pointed to by {\ttfamily dst}, where {\ttfamily kind} specifies the direction of the copy, and must be one of cuda\+Memcpy\+Host\+To\+Host, cuda\+Memcpy\+Host\+To\+Device, cuda\+Memcpy\+Device\+To\+Host, cuda\+Memcpy\+Device\+To\+Device, or \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Default}. Passing \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Default} is recommended, in which case the type of transfer is inferred from the pointer values. However, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Default} is only allowed on systems that support unified virtual addressing.

The memory areas may not overlap. Calling \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gafb6d05d580838d8efbe581ca69cd7ac7}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Async()} with {\ttfamily dst} and {\ttfamily src} pointers that do not match the direction of the copy results in an undefined behavior.

\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gafb6d05d580838d8efbe581ca69cd7ac7}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Async()} is asynchronous with respect to the host, so the call may return before the copy is complete. The copy can optionally be associated to a stream by passing a non-\/zero {\ttfamily stream} argument. If {\ttfamily kind} is cuda\+Memcpy\+Host\+To\+Device or cuda\+Memcpy\+Device\+To\+Host and the {\ttfamily stream} is non-\/zero, the copy may overlap with operations in other streams.

The device version of this function only handles device to device copies and cannot be given local or shared pointers.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em dst} & -\/ Destination memory address \\
\hline
{\em src} & -\/ Source memory address \\
\hline
{\em count} & -\/ Size in bytes to copy \\
\hline
{\em kind} & -\/ Type of transfer \\
\hline
{\em stream} & -\/ Stream identifier\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
cuda\+Success, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Memcpy\+Direction \textbackslash{}notefnerr \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+async \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+null\+\_\+stream \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+init\+\_\+rt \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+callback \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+memcpy
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaMemcpyFromSymbol()}{cudaMemcpyFromSymbol()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Memcpy\+From\+Symbol (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{dst,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{symbol,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{count,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}} offset }]{\+\_\+\+\_\+dv0,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{enum}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga8ce1ad49a1e77a595edcb25ac795cd0f}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Kind}} kind }]{\+\_\+\+\_\+dvcuda\+Memcpy\+Device\+To\+Host }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Copies data from the given symbol on the device. 

Copies {\ttfamily count} bytes from the memory area pointed to by {\ttfamily offset} bytes from the start of symbol {\ttfamily symbol} to the memory area pointed to by {\ttfamily dst}. The memory areas may not overlap. {\ttfamily symbol} is a variable that resides in global or constant memory space. {\ttfamily kind} can be either cuda\+Memcpy\+Device\+To\+Host, cuda\+Memcpy\+Device\+To\+Device, or \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Default}. Passing \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Default} is recommended, in which case the type of transfer is inferred from the pointer values. However, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Default} is only allowed on systems that support unified virtual addressing.

\hline
{\em symbol} & -\/ Device symbol address \\
\hline
{\em count} & -\/ Size in bytes to copy \\
\hline
{\em offset} & -\/ Offset from start of symbol in bytes \\
\hline
{\em kind} & -\/ Type of transfer\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
cuda\+Success, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Symbol, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Memcpy\+Direction, cuda\+Error\+No\+Kernel\+Image\+For\+Device \textbackslash{}notefnerr \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+sync \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+string\+\_\+api\+\_\+deprecation \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+init\+\_\+rt \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+callback
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaMemcpyFromSymbolAsync()}{cudaMemcpyFromSymbolAsync()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Memcpy\+From\+Symbol\+Async (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{dst,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{symbol,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{count,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{offset,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{enum}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga8ce1ad49a1e77a595edcb25ac795cd0f}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Kind}}}]{kind,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gae6a6dd5bf3109046a07da4b735234e81}{cuda\+Stream\+\_\+t}} stream }]{\+\_\+\+\_\+dv0 }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Copies data from the given symbol on the device. 

Copies {\ttfamily count} bytes from the memory area pointed to by {\ttfamily offset} bytes from the start of symbol {\ttfamily symbol} to the memory area pointed to by {\ttfamily dst}. The memory areas may not overlap. {\ttfamily symbol} is a variable that resides in global or constant memory space. {\ttfamily kind} can be either cuda\+Memcpy\+Device\+To\+Host, cuda\+Memcpy\+Device\+To\+Device, or \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Default}. Passing \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Default} is recommended, in which case the type of transfer is inferred from the pointer values. However, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Default} is only allowed on systems that support unified virtual addressing.

\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga4be8411d879e1ed4589da65c87d99857}{cuda\+Memcpy\+From\+Symbol\+Async()} is asynchronous with respect to the host, so the call may return before the copy is complete. The copy can optionally be associated to a stream by passing a non-\/zero {\ttfamily stream} argument. If {\ttfamily kind} is cuda\+Memcpy\+Device\+To\+Host and {\ttfamily stream} is non-\/zero, the copy may overlap with operations in other streams.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em dst} & -\/ Destination memory address \\
\hline
{\em symbol} & -\/ Device symbol address \\
\hline
{\em count} & -\/ Size in bytes to copy \\
\hline
{\em offset} & -\/ Offset from start of symbol in bytes \\
\hline
{\em kind} & -\/ Type of transfer \\
\hline
{\em stream} & -\/ Stream identifier\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

cuda\+Success, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Symbol, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Memcpy\+Direction, cuda\+Error\+No\+Kernel\+Image\+For\+Device \textbackslash{}notefnerr \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+async \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+null\+\_\+stream \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+string\+\_\+api\+\_\+deprecation \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+init\+\_\+rt \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+callback
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaMemcpyPeer()}{cudaMemcpyPeer()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Memcpy\+Peer (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{dst,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{int}}}]{dst\+Device,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{src,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{int}}}]{src\+Device,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{count }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Copies memory between two devices. 

Copies memory from one device to memory on another device. {\ttfamily dst} is the base device pointer of the destination memory and {\ttfamily dst\+Device} is the destination device. {\ttfamily src} is the base device pointer of the source memory and {\ttfamily src\+Device} is the source device. {\ttfamily count} specifies the number of bytes to copy.

Note that this function is asynchronous with respect to the host, but serialized with respect all pending and future asynchronous work in to the current device, {\ttfamily src\+Device}, and {\ttfamily dst\+Device} (use \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga798259a9743470a89bfbe225a195771b}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Peer\+Async} to avoid this synchronization).


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em dst} & -\/ Destination device pointer \\
\hline
{\em dst\+Device} & -\/ Destination device \\
\hline
{\em src} & -\/ Source device pointer \\
\hline
{\em src\+Device} & -\/ Source device \\
\hline
{\em count} & -\/ Size of memory copy in bytes\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
cuda\+Success, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Device \textbackslash{}notefnerr \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+sync \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+init\+\_\+rt \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+callback
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaMemcpyPeerAsync()}{cudaMemcpyPeerAsync()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Memcpy\+Peer\+Async (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{dst,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{int}}}]{dst\+Device,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{src,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{int}}}]{src\+Device,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{count,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gae6a6dd5bf3109046a07da4b735234e81}{cuda\+Stream\+\_\+t}} stream }]{\+\_\+\+\_\+dv0 }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Copies memory between two devices asynchronously. 

Copies memory from one device to memory on another device. {\ttfamily dst} is the base device pointer of the destination memory and {\ttfamily dst\+Device} is the destination device. {\ttfamily src} is the base device pointer of the source memory and {\ttfamily src\+Device} is the source device. {\ttfamily count} specifies the number of bytes to copy.

Note that this function is asynchronous with respect to the host and all work on other devices.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaMemcpyToSymbol()}{cudaMemcpyToSymbol()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Memcpy\+To\+Symbol (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{symbol,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{src,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{count,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}} offset }]{\+\_\+\+\_\+dv0,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{enum}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga8ce1ad49a1e77a595edcb25ac795cd0f}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Kind}} kind }]{\+\_\+\+\_\+dvcuda\+Memcpy\+Host\+To\+Device }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Copies data to the given symbol on the device. 

Copies {\ttfamily count} bytes from the memory area pointed to by {\ttfamily src} to the memory area pointed to by {\ttfamily offset} bytes from the start of symbol {\ttfamily symbol}. The memory areas may not overlap. {\ttfamily symbol} is a variable that resides in global or constant memory space. {\ttfamily kind} can be either cuda\+Memcpy\+Host\+To\+Device, cuda\+Memcpy\+Device\+To\+Device, or \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Default}. Passing \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Default} is recommended, in which case the type of transfer is inferred from the pointer values. However, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Default} is only allowed on systems that support unified virtual addressing.

\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gae2bbb87e03bde890140dae4b348e1886}{cuda\+Memcpy}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gadf7361e67d7228dbb554f1ccb47d54b1}{cuda\+Memcpy2D}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga6ea4e52dd6157f45425fdcff3f6d9d3d}{cuda\+Memcpy2\+DTo\+Array}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga94a63ef65830ce0c5a8bc8b8208caacb}{cuda\+Memcpy2\+DFrom\+Array}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gac8f08a316c1b641bb7ecc85012ddf25d}{cuda\+Memcpy2\+DArray\+To\+Array}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga9356cb69eef5a12c7ea255c1b010f121}{cuda\+Memcpy\+From\+Symbol}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gafb6d05d580838d8efbe581ca69cd7ac7}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Async}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga18f73e4d8f45009a3a733407b0ab5fbf}{cuda\+Memcpy2\+DAsync}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga5e33c77f7fe3cbc1add4671604c30b7d}{cuda\+Memcpy2\+DTo\+Array\+Async}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gae66d22de38a11ce8e09f8f788b2cf275}{cuda\+Memcpy2\+DFrom\+Array\+Async}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga6110c29da79fc76851d202e27de9aa2c}{cuda\+Memcpy\+To\+Symbol\+Async}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga4be8411d879e1ed4589da65c87d99857}{cuda\+Memcpy\+From\+Symbol\+Async}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___m_e_m_ga80d68f9149eba8f5d42a19fbe967c353}{cu\+Memcpy}, cu\+Memcpy\+HtoD, cu\+Memcpy\+DtoD

\index{Memory Management@{Memory Management}!cudaMemcpyToSymbolAsync@{cudaMemcpyToSymbolAsync}}
\index{cudaMemcpyToSymbolAsync@{cudaMemcpyToSymbolAsync}!Memory Management@{Memory Management}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaMemcpyToSymbolAsync()}{cudaMemcpyToSymbolAsync()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Memcpy\+To\+Symbol\+Async (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{symbol,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{src,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{count,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{offset,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{enum}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga8ce1ad49a1e77a595edcb25ac795cd0f}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Kind}}}]{kind,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gae6a6dd5bf3109046a07da4b735234e81}{cuda\+Stream\+\_\+t}} stream }]{\+\_\+\+\_\+dv0 }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Copies data to the given symbol on the device. 

Copies {\ttfamily count} bytes from the memory area pointed to by {\ttfamily src} to the memory area pointed to by {\ttfamily offset} bytes from the start of symbol {\ttfamily symbol}. The memory areas may not overlap. {\ttfamily symbol} is a variable that resides in global or constant memory space. {\ttfamily kind} can be either cuda\+Memcpy\+Host\+To\+Device, cuda\+Memcpy\+Device\+To\+Device, or \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Default}. Passing \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Default} is recommended, in which case the type of transfer is inferred from the pointer values. However, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Default} is only allowed on systems that support unified virtual addressing.

\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga6110c29da79fc76851d202e27de9aa2c}{cuda\+Memcpy\+To\+Symbol\+Async()} is asynchronous with respect to the host, so the call may return before the copy is complete. The copy can optionally be associated to a stream by passing a non-\/zero {\ttfamily stream} argument. If {\ttfamily kind} is cuda\+Memcpy\+Host\+To\+Device and {\ttfamily stream} is non-\/zero, the copy may overlap with operations in other streams.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}

\hline
{\em src} & -\/ Source memory address \\
\hline
{\em count} & -\/ Size in bytes to copy \\
\hline
{\em offset} & -\/ Offset from start of symbol in bytes \\
\hline
{\em kind} & -\/ Type of transfer \\
\hline
{\em stream} & -\/ Stream identifier\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\end{DoxyReturn}

\Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gad5dad131be512b949e362a169eed7be2}\label{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gad5dad131be512b949e362a169eed7be2} 
\index{Memory Management@{Memory Management}!cudaMemGetInfo@{cudaMemGetInfo}}
\index{cudaMemGetInfo@{cudaMemGetInfo}!Memory Management@{Memory Management}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaMemGetInfo()}{cudaMemGetInfo()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Mem\+Get\+Info (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{free,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{total }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Gets free and total device memory. 

Returns in {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}total} the total amount of memory available to the the current context. Returns in {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}free} the amount of memory on the device that is free according to the OS. CUDA is not guaranteed to be able to allocate all of the memory that the OS reports as free. In a multi-\/tenet situation, free estimate returned is prone to race condition where a new allocation/free done by a different process or a different thread in the same process between the time when free memory was estimated and reported, will result in deviation in free value reported and actual free memory.

The integrated GPU on Tegra shares memory with CPU and other component of the SoC. The free and total values returned by the API excludes the SWAP memory space maintained by the OS on some platforms. The OS may move some of the memory pages into swap area as the GPU or CPU allocate or access memory. See Tegra app note on how to calculate total and free memory on Tegra.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em free} & -\/ Returned free memory in bytes \\
\hline
{\em total} & -\/ Returned total memory in bytes\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\end{DoxyReturn}

\Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga4a666ced2163d18849c59c608bfbd208}\label{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga4a666ced2163d18849c59c608bfbd208} 
\index{Memory Management@{Memory Management}!cudaMemPrefetchAsync@{cudaMemPrefetchAsync}}
\index{cudaMemPrefetchAsync@{cudaMemPrefetchAsync}!Memory Management@{Memory Management}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaMemPrefetchAsync()}{cudaMemPrefetchAsync()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Mem\+Prefetch\+Async (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{dev\+Ptr,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{count,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{int}}}]{dst\+Device,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gae6a6dd5bf3109046a07da4b735234e81}{cuda\+Stream\+\_\+t}} stream }]{\+\_\+\+\_\+dv0 }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Prefetches memory to the specified destination device. 

Prefetches memory to the specified destination device. {\ttfamily dev\+Ptr} is the base device pointer of the memory to be prefetched and {\ttfamily dst\+Device} is the destination device. {\ttfamily count} specifies the number of bytes to copy. {\ttfamily stream} is the stream in which the operation is enqueued. The memory range must refer to managed memory allocated via \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gac85541d7e0fa6bdaeed967fee1c8e780}{cuda\+Malloc\+Managed} or declared via {\bfseries{managed}} variables.

Passing in cuda\+Cpu\+Device\+Id for {\ttfamily dst\+Device} will prefetch the data to host memory. If {\ttfamily dst\+Device} is a GPU, then the device attribute cuda\+Dev\+Attr\+Concurrent\+Managed\+Access must be non-\/zero. Additionally, {\ttfamily stream} must be associated with a device that has a non-\/zero value for the device attribute cuda\+Dev\+Attr\+Concurrent\+Managed\+Access.

The start address and end address of the memory range will be rounded down and rounded up respectively to be aligned to CPU page size before the prefetch operation is enqueued in the stream.

If no physical memory has been allocated for this region, then this memory region will be populated and mapped on the destination device. If there\textquotesingle{}s insufficient memory to prefetch the desired region, the Unified Memory driver may evict pages from other \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gac85541d7e0fa6bdaeed967fee1c8e780}{cuda\+Malloc\+Managed} allocations to host memory in order to make room. Device memory allocated using \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga2ec57cea7c57e8e3c4beca43dd327134}{cuda\+Malloc} or \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gaae428013daae74529feb93b48a9dc39b}{cuda\+Malloc\+Array} will not be evicted.

By default, any mappings to the previous location of the migrated pages are removed and mappings for the new location are only setup on {\ttfamily dst\+Device}. The exact behavior however also depends on the settings applied to this memory range via \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gac45d3db8ba1c1387396174838fd7dfad}{cuda\+Mem\+Advise} as described below\+:

If cuda\+Mem\+Advise\+Set\+Read\+Mostly was set on any subset of this memory range, then that subset will create a read-\/only copy of the pages on {\ttfamily dst\+Device}.

If cuda\+Mem\+Advise\+Set\+Preferred\+Location was called on any subset of this memory range, then the pages will be migrated to {\ttfamily dst\+Device} even if {\ttfamily dst\+Device} is not the preferred location of any pages in the memory range.

If cuda\+Mem\+Advise\+Set\+Accessed\+By was called on any subset of this memory range, then mappings to those pages from all the appropriate processors are updated to refer to the new location if establishing such a mapping is possible. Otherwise, those mappings are cleared.

Note that this API is not required for functionality and only serves to improve performance by allowing the application to migrate data to a suitable location before it is accessed. Memory accesses to this range are always coherent and are allowed even when the data is actively being migrated.

Note that this function is asynchronous with respect to the host and all work on other devices.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em dev\+Ptr} & -\/ Pointer to be prefetched \\
\hline
{\em count} & -\/ Size in bytes \\
\hline
{\em dst\+Device} & -\/ Destination device to prefetch to \\
\hline
{\em stream} & -\/ Stream to enqueue prefetch operation\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
cuda\+Success, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Device \textbackslash{}notefnerr \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+async \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+null\+\_\+stream \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+init\+\_\+rt \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+callback
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gae2bbb87e03bde890140dae4b348e1886}{cuda\+Memcpy}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga78c39ede7a1455e7d375dbad8f2bc5cc}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Peer}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gafb6d05d580838d8efbe581ca69cd7ac7}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Async}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga5fbe9d79a247ae6de5729c9e78721241}{cuda\+Memcpy3\+DPeer\+Async}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gac45d3db8ba1c1387396174838fd7dfad}{cuda\+Mem\+Advise}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___u_n_i_f_i_e_d_gaa6237bda35679c3b6b2bb6e0fe8126d3}{cu\+Mem\+Prefetch\+Async} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gae5f23e2e3bfb47692ccdd2bdc69c8ae3}\label{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gae5f23e2e3bfb47692ccdd2bdc69c8ae3} 
\index{Memory Management@{Memory Management}!cudaMemRangeGetAttribute@{cudaMemRangeGetAttribute}}
\index{cudaMemRangeGetAttribute@{cudaMemRangeGetAttribute}!Memory Management@{Memory Management}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaMemRangeGetAttribute()}{cudaMemRangeGetAttribute()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Mem\+Range\+Get\+Attribute (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{data,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{data\+Size,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{enum}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga2fe31b7bc95548a9355af5817cfa83ae}{cuda\+Mem\+Range\+Attribute}}}]{attribute,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{dev\+Ptr,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{count }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Query an attribute of a given memory range. 

Query an attribute about the memory range starting at {\ttfamily dev\+Ptr} with a size of {\ttfamily count} bytes. The memory range must refer to managed memory allocated via \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gac85541d7e0fa6bdaeed967fee1c8e780}{cuda\+Malloc\+Managed} or declared via {\bfseries{managed}} variables.

The {\ttfamily attribute} parameter can take the following values\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Mem\+Range\+Attribute\+Read\+Mostly\+:} If this attribute is specified, {\ttfamily data} will be interpreted as a 32-\/bit integer, and {\ttfamily data\+Size} must be 4. The result returned will be 1 if all pages in the given memory range have read-\/duplication enabled, or 0 otherwise.
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Mem\+Range\+Attribute\+Preferred\+Location\+:} If this attribute is specified, {\ttfamily data} will be interpreted as a 32-\/bit integer, and {\ttfamily data\+Size} must be 4. The result returned will be a GPU device id if all pages in the memory range have that GPU as their preferred location, or it will be cuda\+Cpu\+Device\+Id if all pages in the memory range have the CPU as their preferred location, or it will be cuda\+Invalid\+Device\+Id if either all the pages don\textquotesingle{}t have the same preferred location or some of the pages don\textquotesingle{}t have a preferred location at all. Note that the actual location of the pages in the memory range at the time of the query may be different from the preferred location.
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Mem\+Range\+Attribute\+Accessed\+By\+:} If this attribute is specified, {\ttfamily data} will be interpreted as an array of 32-\/bit integers, and {\ttfamily data\+Size} must be a non-\/zero multiple of 4. The result returned will be a list of device ids that had \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Mem\+Advice\+Set\+Accessed\+By} set for that entire memory range. If any device does not have that advice set for the entire memory range, that device will not be included. If {\ttfamily data} is larger than the number of devices that have that advice set for that memory range, cuda\+Invalid\+Device\+Id will be returned in all the extra space provided. For ex., if {\ttfamily data\+Size} is 12 (i.\+e. {\ttfamily data} has 3 elements) and only device 0 has the advice set, then the result returned will be \{ 0, cuda\+Invalid\+Device\+Id, cuda\+Invalid\+Device\+Id \}. If {\ttfamily data} is smaller than the number of devices that have that advice set, then only as many devices will be returned as can fit in the array. There is no guarantee on which specific devices will be returned, however.
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Mem\+Range\+Attribute\+Last\+Prefetch\+Location\+:} If this attribute is specified, {\ttfamily data} will be interpreted as a 32-\/bit integer, and {\ttfamily data\+Size} must be 4. The result returned will be the last location to which all pages in the memory range were prefetched explicitly via \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga4a666ced2163d18849c59c608bfbd208}{cuda\+Mem\+Prefetch\+Async}. This will either be a GPU id or cuda\+Cpu\+Device\+Id depending on whether the last location for prefetch was a GPU or the CPU respectively. If any page in the memory range was never explicitly prefetched or if all pages were not prefetched to the same location, cuda\+Invalid\+Device\+Id will be returned. Note that this simply returns the last location that the applicaton requested to prefetch the memory range to. It gives no indication as to whether the prefetch operation to that location has completed or even begun.
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em data} & -\/ A pointers to a memory location where the result of each attribute query will be written to. \\
\hline
{\em data\+Size} & -\/ Array containing the size of data \\
\hline
{\em attribute} & -\/ The attribute to query \\
\hline
{\em dev\+Ptr} & -\/ Start of the range to query \\
\hline
{\em count} & -\/ Size of the range to query\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

cuda\+Success, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value \textbackslash{}notefnerr \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+async \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+null\+\_\+stream \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+init\+\_\+rt \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+callback
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gad5038f91ff2105b6a4744968eaf626b1}{cuda\+Mem\+Range\+Get\+Attributes}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga4a666ced2163d18849c59c608bfbd208}{cuda\+Mem\+Prefetch\+Async}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gac45d3db8ba1c1387396174838fd7dfad}{cuda\+Mem\+Advise}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___u_n_i_f_i_e_d_ga5fed71a86ab1a0066edad299a61f3828}{cu\+Mem\+Range\+Get\+Attribute} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaMemRangeGetAttributes()}{cudaMemRangeGetAttributes()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Mem\+Range\+Get\+Attributes (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{data,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{data\+Sizes,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{enum}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga2fe31b7bc95548a9355af5817cfa83ae}{cuda\+Mem\+Range\+Attribute}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{attributes,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{num\+Attributes,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{dev\+Ptr,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{count }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Query attributes of a given memory range. 

Query attributes of the memory range starting at {\ttfamily dev\+Ptr} with a size of {\ttfamily count} bytes. The memory range must refer to managed memory allocated via \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gac85541d7e0fa6bdaeed967fee1c8e780}{cuda\+Malloc\+Managed} or declared via {\bfseries{managed}} variables. The {\ttfamily attributes} array will be interpreted to have {\ttfamily num\+Attributes} entries. The {\ttfamily data\+Sizes} array will also be interpreted to have {\ttfamily num\+Attributes} entries. The results of the query will be stored in {\ttfamily data}.

The list of supported attributes are given below. Please refer to \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gae5f23e2e3bfb47692ccdd2bdc69c8ae3}{cuda\+Mem\+Range\+Get\+Attribute} for attribute descriptions and restrictions.


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item cuda\+Mem\+Range\+Attribute\+Read\+Mostly
\item cuda\+Mem\+Range\+Attribute\+Preferred\+Location
\item cuda\+Mem\+Range\+Attribute\+Accessed\+By
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Mem\+Range\+Attribute\+Last\+Prefetch\+Location}
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em data} & -\/ A two-\/dimensional array containing pointers to memory locations where the result of each attribute query will be written to. \\
\hline
{\em data\+Sizes} & -\/ Array containing the sizes of each result \\
\hline
{\em attributes} & -\/ An array of attributes to query (num\+Attributes and the number of attributes in this array should match) \\
\hline
{\em num\+Attributes} & -\/ Number of attributes to query \\
\hline
{\em dev\+Ptr} & -\/ Start of the range to query \\
\hline
{\em count} & -\/ Size of the range to query\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
cuda\+Success, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value \textbackslash{}notefnerr \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+init\+\_\+rt \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+callback
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaMemset()}{cudaMemset()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Memset (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{dev\+Ptr,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{int}}}]{value,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{count }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Initializes or sets device memory to a value. 

Fills the first {\ttfamily count} bytes of the memory area pointed to by {\ttfamily dev\+Ptr} with the constant byte value {\ttfamily value}.

Note that this function is asynchronous with respect to the host unless {\ttfamily dev\+Ptr} refers to pinned host memory.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}

\hline
{\em value} & -\/ Value to set for each byte of specified memory \\

\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaMemset2D()}{cudaMemset2D()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Memset2D (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{dev\+Ptr,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{pitch,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{int}}}]{value,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{width,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{height }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Initializes or sets device memory to a value. 

Sets to the specified value {\ttfamily value} a matrix ({\ttfamily height} rows of {\ttfamily width} bytes each) pointed to by {\ttfamily dst\+Ptr}. {\ttfamily pitch} is the width in bytes of the 2D array pointed to by {\ttfamily dst\+Ptr}, including any padding added to the end of each row. This function performs fastest when the pitch is one that has been passed back by \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gafba768d1a49ed27c0672832403544252}{cuda\+Malloc\+Pitch()}.

Note that this function is asynchronous with respect to the host unless {\ttfamily dev\+Ptr} refers to pinned host memory.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em dev\+Ptr} & -\/ Pointer to 2D device memory \\
\hline
{\em pitch} & -\/ Pitch in bytes of 2D device memory(Unused if {\ttfamily height} is 1) \\
\hline
{\em value} & -\/ Value to set for each byte of specified memory \\
\hline
{\em width} & -\/ Width of matrix set (columns in bytes) \\
\hline
{\em height} & -\/ Height of matrix set (rows)\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
cuda\+Success, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value, \textbackslash{}notefnerr \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+memset \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+init\+\_\+rt \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+callback
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaMemset2DAsync()}{cudaMemset2DAsync()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+cudart\+\_\+builtin\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Memset2\+DAsync (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{dev\+Ptr,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{pitch,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{int}}}]{value,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{width,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{height,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gae6a6dd5bf3109046a07da4b735234e81}{cuda\+Stream\+\_\+t}} stream }]{\+\_\+\+\_\+dv0 }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Initializes or sets device memory to a value. 

Sets to the specified value {\ttfamily value} a matrix ({\ttfamily height} rows of {\ttfamily width} bytes each) pointed to by {\ttfamily dst\+Ptr}. {\ttfamily pitch} is the width in bytes of the 2D array pointed to by {\ttfamily dst\+Ptr}, including any padding added to the end of each row. This function performs fastest when the pitch is one that has been passed back by \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gafba768d1a49ed27c0672832403544252}{cuda\+Malloc\+Pitch()}.

\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga4c232d19be6f54dcd2579dae3b962f12}{cuda\+Memset2\+DAsync()} is asynchronous with respect to the host, so the call may return before the memset is complete. The operation can optionally be associated to a stream by passing a non-\/zero {\ttfamily stream} argument. If {\ttfamily stream} is non-\/zero, the operation may overlap with operations in other streams.

The device version of this function only handles device to device copies and cannot be given local or shared pointers.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em dev\+Ptr} & -\/ Pointer to 2D device memory \\
\hline
{\em pitch} & -\/ Pitch in bytes of 2D device memory(Unused if {\ttfamily height} is 1) \\
\hline
{\em value} & -\/ Value to set for each byte of specified memory \\
\hline
{\em width} & -\/ Width of matrix set (columns in bytes) \\
\hline
{\em height} & -\/ Height of matrix set (rows) \\
\hline
{\em stream} & -\/ Stream identifier\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
cuda\+Success, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value, \textbackslash{}notefnerr \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+memset \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+null\+\_\+stream \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+init\+\_\+rt \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+callback
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{Memory Management@{Memory Management}!cudaMemset3D@{cudaMemset3D}}
\index{cudaMemset3D@{cudaMemset3D}!Memory Management@{Memory Management}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaMemset3D()}{cudaMemset3D()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Memset3D (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{struct}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structcuda_pitched_ptr}{cuda\+Pitched\+Ptr}}}]{pitched\+Dev\+Ptr,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{int}}}]{value,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{struct}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structcuda_extent}{cuda\+Extent}}}]{extent }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Initializes or sets device memory to a value. 

Initializes each element of a 3D array to the specified value {\ttfamily value}. The object to initialize is defined by {\ttfamily pitched\+Dev\+Ptr}. The {\ttfamily pitch} field of {\ttfamily pitched\+Dev\+Ptr} is the width in memory in bytes of the 3D array pointed to by {\ttfamily pitched\+Dev\+Ptr}, including any padding added to the end of each row. The {\ttfamily xsize} field specifies the logical width of each row in bytes, while the {\ttfamily ysize} field specifies the height of each 2D slice in rows. The {\ttfamily pitch} field of {\ttfamily pitched\+Dev\+Ptr} is ignored when {\ttfamily height} and {\ttfamily depth} are both equal to 1.

The extents of the initialized region are specified as a {\ttfamily width} in bytes, a {\ttfamily height} in rows, and a {\ttfamily depth} in slices.

Extents with {\ttfamily width} greater than or equal to the {\ttfamily xsize} of {\ttfamily pitched\+Dev\+Ptr} may perform significantly faster than extents narrower than the {\ttfamily xsize}. Secondarily, extents with {\ttfamily height} equal to the {\ttfamily ysize} of {\ttfamily pitched\+Dev\+Ptr} will perform faster than when the {\ttfamily height} is shorter than the {\ttfamily ysize}.

This function performs fastest when the {\ttfamily pitched\+Dev\+Ptr} has been allocated by \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga38d900061e670e541cebf5042e0e7739}{cuda\+Malloc3\+D()}.

Note that this function is asynchronous with respect to the host unless {\ttfamily pitched\+Dev\+Ptr} refers to pinned host memory.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em pitched\+Dev\+Ptr} & -\/ Pointer to pitched device memory \\
\hline
{\em value} & -\/ Value to set for each byte of specified memory \\
\hline
{\em extent} & -\/ Size parameters for where to set device memory ({\ttfamily width} field in bytes)\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
cuda\+Success, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value, \textbackslash{}notefnerr \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+memset \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+init\+\_\+rt \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+callback
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}

\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaMemset3DAsync()}{cudaMemset3DAsync()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+cudart\+\_\+builtin\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Memset3\+DAsync (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{struct}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structcuda_pitched_ptr}{cuda\+Pitched\+Ptr}}}]{pitched\+Dev\+Ptr,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{int}}}]{value,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{struct}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structcuda_extent}{cuda\+Extent}}}]{extent,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gae6a6dd5bf3109046a07da4b735234e81}{cuda\+Stream\+\_\+t}} stream }]{\+\_\+\+\_\+dv0 }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Initializes or sets device memory to a value. 

Initializes each element of a 3D array to the specified value {\ttfamily value}. The object to initialize is defined by {\ttfamily pitched\+Dev\+Ptr}. The {\ttfamily pitch} field of {\ttfamily pitched\+Dev\+Ptr} is the width in memory in bytes of the 3D array pointed to by {\ttfamily pitched\+Dev\+Ptr}, including any padding added to the end of each row. The {\ttfamily xsize} field specifies the logical width of each row in bytes, while the {\ttfamily ysize} field specifies the height of each 2D slice in rows. The {\ttfamily pitch} field of {\ttfamily pitched\+Dev\+Ptr} is ignored when {\ttfamily height} and {\ttfamily depth} are both equal to 1.

The extents of the initialized region are specified as a {\ttfamily width} in bytes, a {\ttfamily height} in rows, and a {\ttfamily depth} in slices.

Extents with {\ttfamily width} greater than or equal to the {\ttfamily xsize} of {\ttfamily pitched\+Dev\+Ptr} may perform significantly faster than extents narrower than the {\ttfamily xsize}. Secondarily, extents with {\ttfamily height} equal to the {\ttfamily ysize} of {\ttfamily pitched\+Dev\+Ptr} will perform faster than when the {\ttfamily height} is shorter than the {\ttfamily ysize}.

This function performs fastest when the {\ttfamily pitched\+Dev\+Ptr} has been allocated by \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga38d900061e670e541cebf5042e0e7739}{cuda\+Malloc3\+D()}.

\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gab8c24ee1437c07cee8686da0e98015e2}{cuda\+Memset3\+DAsync()} is asynchronous with respect to the host, so the call may return before the memset is complete. The operation can optionally be associated to a stream by passing a non-\/zero {\ttfamily stream} argument. If {\ttfamily stream} is non-\/zero, the operation may overlap with operations in other streams.

The device version of this function only handles device to device copies and cannot be given local or shared pointers.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+cudart\+\_\+builtin\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Memset\+Async (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{dev\+Ptr,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{int}}}]{value,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{count,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gae6a6dd5bf3109046a07da4b735234e81}{cuda\+Stream\+\_\+t}} stream }]{\+\_\+\+\_\+dv0 }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Initializes or sets device memory to a value. 

Fills the first {\ttfamily count} bytes of the memory area pointed to by {\ttfamily dev\+Ptr} with the constant byte value {\ttfamily value}.

\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gadee9f2369cfbe4b48574c7513fbb06ea}{cuda\+Memset\+Async()} is asynchronous with respect to the host, so the call may return before the memset is complete. The operation can optionally be associated to a stream by passing a non-\/zero {\ttfamily stream} argument. If {\ttfamily stream} is non-\/zero, the operation may overlap with operations in other streams.

The device version of this function only handles device to device copies and cannot be given local or shared pointers.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaMipmappedArrayGetMemoryRequirements()}{cudaMipmappedArrayGetMemoryRequirements()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Mipmapped\+Array\+Get\+Memory\+Requirements (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{struct}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structcuda_array_memory_requirements}{cuda\+Array\+Memory\+Requirements}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{memory\+Requirements,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga1b03ad14fc0ab86f8b033837f5562d8a}{cuda\+Mipmapped\+Array\+\_\+t}}}]{mipmap,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{int}}}]{device }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Returns the memory requirements of a CUDA mipmapped array. 

Returns the memory requirements of a CUDA mipmapped array in {\ttfamily memory\+Requirements} If the CUDA mipmapped array is not allocated with flag \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga91a50795515848406a89c2e6cef2fb02}{cuda\+Array\+Deferred\+Mapping} cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value will be returned.

The returned value in \doxylink{structcuda_array_memory_requirements_acff0bc12daa05c6c40892a2187befd87}{cuda\+Array\+Memory\+Requirements\+::size} represents the total size of the CUDA mipmapped array. The returned value in \doxylink{structcuda_array_memory_requirements_a37898b13b500d39e4a43d0ee04cf0ef3}{cuda\+Array\+Memory\+Requirements\+::alignment} represents the alignment necessary for mapping the CUDA mipmapped array.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
cuda\+Success cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value
\end{DoxyReturn}

\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em device} & -\/ Device to get the memory requirements for \\

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaMipmappedArrayGetSparseProperties()}{cudaMipmappedArrayGetSparseProperties()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Mipmapped\+Array\+Get\+Sparse\+Properties (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{struct}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structcuda_array_sparse_properties}{cuda\+Array\+Sparse\+Properties}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{sparse\+Properties,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga1b03ad14fc0ab86f8b033837f5562d8a}{cuda\+Mipmapped\+Array\+\_\+t}}}]{mipmap }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Returns the layout properties of a sparse CUDA mipmapped array. 

Returns the sparse array layout properties in {\ttfamily sparse\+Properties}. If the CUDA mipmapped array is not allocated with flag \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga42c353686a15da063dc7722594ae4bff}{cuda\+Array\+Sparse} cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value will be returned.

For non-\/layered CUDA mipmapped arrays, \doxylink{structcuda_array_sparse_properties_a22cfa4ad83195f0e9585303c988bb886}{cuda\+Array\+Sparse\+Properties\+::miptail\+Size} returns the size of the mip tail region. The mip tail region includes all mip levels whose width, height or depth is less than that of the tile. For layered CUDA mipmapped arrays, if \doxylink{structcuda_array_sparse_properties_a44c8728469d60e511aceb4ba7086c164}{cuda\+Array\+Sparse\+Properties\+::flags} contains \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga6820071ffa1300699897eab8d319e4d9}{cuda\+Array\+Sparse\+Properties\+Single\+Mip\+Tail}, then \doxylink{structcuda_array_sparse_properties_a22cfa4ad83195f0e9585303c988bb886}{cuda\+Array\+Sparse\+Properties\+::miptail\+Size} specifies the size of the mip tail of all layers combined. Otherwise, \doxylink{structcuda_array_sparse_properties_a22cfa4ad83195f0e9585303c988bb886}{cuda\+Array\+Sparse\+Properties\+::miptail\+Size} specifies mip tail size per layer. The returned value of \doxylink{structcuda_array_sparse_properties_ab6909e5db55b866477b6cc16fb02f9d3}{cuda\+Array\+Sparse\+Properties\+::miptail\+First\+Level} is valid only if \doxylink{structcuda_array_sparse_properties_a22cfa4ad83195f0e9585303c988bb886}{cuda\+Array\+Sparse\+Properties\+::miptail\+Size} is non-\/zero.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
cuda\+Success cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value
\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em sparse\+Properties} & -\/ Pointer to return \doxylink{structcuda_array_sparse_properties}{cuda\+Array\+Sparse\+Properties} \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em mipmap} & -\/ The CUDA mipmapped array to get the sparse properties of\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
